## ✅ RESOLVED 2026-07-11 — Diagnostics strip: per-gap dedup, real remediation-PR badge, viewer-visible scores (api + frontend)

Closed the four P3 diagnostics-strip gaps in one pass.

- **Per-gap audit dedup.** `AuditRunner.runAudit` now looks up the project's OPEN task titles once (`openTaskTitles`, non-archived + not-Done) and skips filing a per-gap `ticketPerFinding` ticket whose `${audit.name}: ${gap}` title already exists — re-running the Privacy audit before a gap is fixed no longer spams duplicate tickets. Best-effort (empty set on read failure → prior always-file behaviour). Covered by `privacyDedup.test.ts`.
- **Real remediation-PR badge.** New `remediationStatus.ts` (`deriveRemediation`) joins a project's tasks back to a diagnostic BY TITLE PREFIX (no schema change) and collapses them to a lifecycle state — `none` / `filed` / `pr_open` / `resolved`. `ToolService.getProjectScore` + `getTenantRollup` carry a `remediation` summary on each `ProjectDiagnostic(Summary)` (one task read per rollup/score, inside the existing 5-min read-through cache). `ProjectDiagnosticsStrip` gauges render the true badge (green "Remediation PR opened" / "merged", blue "N tickets filed"), falling back to the gap count when no ticket exists — matching the marketing SOC 2 gauge. Covered by `remediationStatus.test.ts`.
- **Viewer-visible diagnostics.** `GET /api/tools/rollup` + `GET /api/tools/projects/:id/score` relaxed from `requireRole(MANAGER)` → `requireRole(VIEWER)`; read-only diagnostic scores are now visible to every workspace member (running audits + raw finding tickets stay role-gated).
- **Onboarding child-step localization.** `InstallBuilderForceAgents` + `InviteTeamMembers` now route every string through `useTranslations` (`installAgents.*`, `inviteMembers.*`) with real zh/es/fr/de in all 5 catalogs (the three `Wizard*Step` children were already localized). `diagnosticsStrip.*` gained the three remediation labels in all 5 catalogs.
- **Verified.** api `tsgo --noEmit` clean · 7 tool tests pass (dedup + remediation + existing privacy lifecycle) · frontend `tsgo --noEmit` clean for touched files (pre-existing unrelated `useMediaRoom.ts` error remains) · localize-guard passes both components · all 5 catalogs parse.
- **Known follow-up:** the remediation badge (like the existing `gapCount`) can lag task PR-state changes by up to the 5-min score/rollup cache TTL — a task PR merge doesn't actively invalidate `tools:projectscore`/`tools:rollup`. Bounded and consistent with the pre-existing gap-count staleness; logged in the roadmap.

## ✅ RESOLVED 2026-07-11 — Active monitoring: a diagram-overlay monitoring canvas whose breaches auto-start the on-call investigation (api 2026.7.74 · frontend 2026.7.50)

The proactive front-door to incident management — the last loop (reporting + active monitoring). The team uploads a diagram / architecture image, overlays monitor pins on it, and a monitor breach opens an incident that fires the existing on-call → escalation → triage → RCA → Evermind loop. No new response plumbing — monitoring is purely a new incident *source*.

- **Data model (mig 0329).** `monitoring_boards` (an uploaded diagram — R2 image key + natural dimensions), `monitors` (a pin at `pos_x`/`pos_y` 0..1 fractions of the image; type heartbeat | http_check | webhook | metric_threshold | manual; per-monitor `webhook_secret`; `status` ok/breached/unknown; `current_incident_id`), and `monitor_events` (its signal/breach/recovery history).
- **Image upload reuses R2.** No new storage — the frontend uploads via the shared `POST /api/brain/upload` (R2 `UPLOADS`), stores the returned key on the board, and renders it via `GET /api/brain/uploads/<key>`.
- **Breach → incident (idempotent).** `MonitoringService` opens an incident (`source='monitor'`, carrying the monitor's affected-system + severity + escalation policy), pages on-call (`EscalationService.pageInitial`), and dispatches the Incident Manager to triage (`dispatchIncidentTriage`) — one open incident per monitor at a time; recovery notes the incident but leaves closure/RCA to the responder.
- **Monitor evaluation reuses the alerts primitives.** `runMonitorSweep` (frequent `*/5` cron, beside escalation) evaluates heartbeat staleness (`last_signal_at` vs interval), HTTP checks (fetch → non-2xx = breach), and metric thresholds (`evaluateMetric` + `comparatorMatches` from the alerts subsystem — one metric-eval implementation, not two).
- **Inbound signal webhook.** `POST /api/monitor-webhooks/:monitorId` (mounted outside tenant auth, gated by the per-monitor token, tenant resolved from the row) accepts breach/heartbeat signals from Datadog/Grafana/cron/custom tools; a bare ping = healthy heartbeat.
- **Reporting.** `GET /api/monitoring/report` (cached, folds the monitor + incident version tokens) rolls up open incidents, MTTR, breakdowns by severity/system/source, and monitor health.
- **UI.** `/monitoring` page: Boards tab (board grid + the **canvas** — image with absolutely-positioned status-colored monitor pins, click-to-add, drag-to-reposition) with a monitor config SlideOutPanel (type-specific config, signal-URL copy, test-signal, event history, incident link), and a Reporting tab (stat tiles + bar breakdowns). Fully localized (all 5 catalogs, 75-key `monitoring` namespace) + nav group.
- **Verified.** api `tsc --noEmit` clean · `check:schema` (290 tables, 0 new drift) · `check:migrations` (271 files) · frontend `tsgo --noEmit` clean · all 5 catalogs parse with the monitoring namespace.

## ✅ RESOLVED 2026-07-11 — Evermind Studio: automatic pre/post regression chip + delta-contribution provenance (CLOSES the last two Studio follow-ups) (api 2026.7.73 · brain-ui 2026.7.23)

The final two Evermind Studio inspect/validate gaps.

- **Automatic regression check (▲/▼ vs previous version).** New api util `application/llm/evermindEval.ts` (`meanEvalLoss` — mean next-token loss over a held-out set, using `EvermindLM.lossAndBackward`). At each merge the coordinator (`ProjectEvermindCoordinatorDO`) scores the PREVIOUS vs the just-MERGED model on the held-out set of examples taught BEFORE this merge (this batch's examples are appended only afterwards, so a merge never grades its own fit), and records an `EvalPoint {baseLoss,newLoss,delta,evalSize}` (rings `eval`/`evalPoints`). `delta = baseLoss − newLoss` (▲ improved/retained, ▼ regressed). Surfaced honestly: `contributions.eval` → a chip on the **Knowledge Map version stat** (`RegressionBadge` in `EvermindBrainMap`) and beside the **console status pill** (`RegressionChip` in the shared `EvermindConsole`), with a tooltip showing `loss base → new across N prior tasks`. Localized in all 5 catalogs (`evermindBrain.reg*` + `projectEvermind.eval*`, ICU plural on task count).
- **Delta-contribution provenance.** The diff-path `/learn` now accepts an optional `label` (run/ticket) threaded `LearnBody → PendingEntry → RecentEntry` (`dispatchProjectEvermindLearn(..., label)` + route). A pre-diffed weight delta has no text, so the label renders in the same `prompt` slot text memories use — making delta rows inspectable without a UI special-case. (Both in-repo producers — agent-runtime + VSIX — use the text-path, which already carries `prompt` provenance; this closes the diff-path, the only one that lacked it.)
- **Perf/safety:** eval runs once per merge (write path, not per read); the contributions read stays cached + version-token-keyed. Eval is best-effort (never fails a merge) and skipped until a held-out set exists. `contributions.eval` degrades to `null` for pre-existing projects.
- **Tests:** `evermindEval.test.ts` (null on empty, finite positive loss, skips too-short, and an end-to-end direction check — a model adapted on the eval text does not regress on it). 35 project-Evermind tests green; api + frontend + VS Code webview typecheck clean.

## ✅ RESOLVED 2026-07-11 — Incidents close the loop: RCA → Knowledge → Evermind, so the workforce learns and stops repeating incident causes (api 2026.7.72 · frontend 2026.7.49)

The incident subsystem covered response but not *learning*. Now a resolved incident produces durable, reusable learning that actually changes future agent behaviour — the back half of ITIL incident management.

- **RCA / post-mortem → first-class Knowledge article.** New `IncidentService.publishPostmortem` renders a structured RCA (summary, impact, root cause, contributing factors, resolution, what-went-well/wrong, action items) and publishes it through the existing knowledge create→publish→version flow via a new shared `publishKnowledgeDoc` helper — so it is versioned, searchable, and read-acknowledgeable like any SOP. Two new `doc_type`s: `postmortem` and `known_error`. Back-linked both ways: `knowledge_documents.source_incident_id` (mig 0328) ↔ `prod_incidents.postmortem_url`.
- **Action items → remediation tasks.** Each RCA action item is filed as a linked follow-up task (incidentId-tagged), so prevention work is tracked, not lost.
- **Knowledge recall during triage.** New `knowledge.search` MCP tool wraps `recallSops` (widened with an optional `docTypes` param) so an agent finds prior RCAs / known-errors BEFORE diagnosing — a recurring incident resolves from the documented workaround. Triage steering now says "search the knowledge base FIRST".
- **Evermind learn.** On post-mortem, `recordIncidentLearning` distils the incident (root cause / what-went-wrong / resolution) into a lesson and contributes it to the project's Evermind via `dispatchProjectEvermindLearnText`, weighted by severity (sev1 = 3×). Best-effort, project-scoped.
- **Evermind recall grounding (the missing half).** `prepareCloudRun` did NOT inject any Evermind recall. Now EVERY cloud run pulls `buildEvermindLessonsBlock` (via `recallProjectEvermindMemory`) into its prompt — "Prior lessons for this work (past runs & incident post-mortems) — do NOT repeat these causes" — keyed by the task text, so a later task touching the same system surfaces the incident lesson. Closes the loop: incident → RCA → Knowledge → Evermind → grounded into the next task.
- **Agent + human surfaces.** New `incidents.postmortem` MCP tool (cloud-allow-listed) + `POST /api/incidents/:id/postmortem` route; frontend war-room "View RCA" / "Publish RCA" form + `postmortem`/`known_error` knowledge doc-type labels/filters/colors. Fully localized (all 5 catalogs: `incidents.rca.*`, `knowledge.type_*`).
- **Verified.** api `tsc --noEmit` clean · `check:schema` (287 tables, 0 new drift) · `check:migrations` (270 files, renumbered 0327→0328 after a concurrent collision) · builtinMcpService (25) + itsmIngest (3) suites green · frontend `tsgo --noEmit` clean · all 5 catalogs parse with the new keys.

---

## ✅ RESOLVED 2026-07-11 — Manager TYPES (Dev/QA/Service Desk/DevOps) + human→manager Coaching Session (api 2026.7.71 · frontend 2026.7.48)

The AI Manager is a designated team member (agent/human/system) that grooms the backlog; two additions make it a domain-aware, directable role rather than one generic bot. Both ride ONE mechanism — a **composite directive** the pass feeds to its AI scoring: `managerType.directive` + active **coaching directives** + the designated agent's persona (`ManagerService.runManagerForProject`).

- **Manager types (functional role)** — new data-driven registry [`managerTypes.ts`](./api/src/application/manager/managerTypes.ts) (`general` | `delivery`=Development | `qa` | `service_desk` | `devops`, extensible), each expressed as a scoring/prioritization `directive` (prompt text). `manager_type` column on `project_manager_configs` (mig 0327); threaded through `ManagerConfigRow` / `EffectiveManagerPolicy` / `resolveEffectiveManagerPolicy` (`normalizeManagerType` fallback). So a "QA manager" values defects/coverage/release-blockers while a "DevOps manager" values deploys/reliability — same mechanical pass, different judgement. Surfaced as the manager's **role** selector on the Manager tab.
- **Coaching Session (human directs the manager)** — new `manager_directives` table (mig 0327; project-scoped OR `project_id NULL` = tenant-wide, matching a manager that manages the whole tenant) + [`managerDirectives.ts`](./api/src/application/manager/managerDirectives.ts). `runManagerForProject` loads active directives (own + tenant-wide, un-expired) and folds them into the composite directive, so coaching actually steers scoring/prioritization on every pass. Entry points: `POST /api/manager/:projectId/coach` (+ `GET /directives`, `PATCH /directives/:id` to retire) AND the **`manager.coach` MCP tool** ([builtinMcpService.ts](./api/src/application/llm/builtinMcpService.ts)) so chatting with the manager in web Brain / VSIX writes to the SAME directive store (`source` = coach|chat). Coaching journals to the manager feed + unified `activity_log` (`manager.coach`).
- **Web** — Manager tab gained a **role selector** (localized type labels/descriptions) + a **Coaching panel** (guidance box, project/workspace scope, live active-directives list with dismiss). `manager.type.*` + `manager.coaching.*` i18n in all 5 catalogs.
- **Verified** — api (manager subset) + frontend typecheck clean; manager + migration tests green (30); schema-drift passes (287 tables incl. `manager_directives`); all 5 catalogs parse.
- **Follow-ups (ROADMAP):** tie `managerType` to the shared workforce role catalog; a coaching-turn option to spawn a discrete manager task (not only a directive); directive expiry/done UI. (Also logged: an unrelated `evermindEmbed.ts` tsc break, not from this work.)



Three fixes from a failed Brain transcript (context-exhausted "LOOP EXHAUSTED", driven by weak flash models):

- **A — agentic coding-model floor.** `reorderPoolForCoding` (`api/src/application/llm/LlmProxyService.ts`) now SOFT-DEMOTES a curated `WEAK_FLASH_CODERS` set (`deepseek/deepseek-v4-flash`, `minimaxai/minimax-m2.7`, `minimax/minimax-m2.5:free`, `@cf/qwen/qwen3-30b-a3b-fp8`, `@cf/meta/llama-3.3-70b-instruct-fp8-fast`) behind stronger coders on any agentic (`hasTools`) auto-select — via a 3-way `codingLeadRank` (strong coder → weak-flash coder → non-coder). Never REMOVES them (never-empty invariant; a Free tenant with only flash coders still reaches them), no free-budget-count change (pure permutation), strict pins bypass entirely, and the strong big-window `@cf/zai-org/glm-4.7-flash` is deliberately kept. Tests: `reorderPoolForCoding.test.ts`.
- **B — auto-compaction before exhaustion (both Brain loops).** (1) server `BrainService.agentReply` runs `compactMessages(convo, CLOUD_COMPACT_DEFAULTS, buildGatewaySummarizer(env))` before each turn (mirrors `cloudAgentEngine`). (2) the embedded `brainRunStore.ts runLoop` (the actual "LOOP EXHAUSTED" path) now SUMMARIZES the older middle into a memoized memory note (client-side summarizer built from the injected `stream` fn) instead of DROPPING oldest turns — pure, tool-pairing-safe helpers `compactTailStart`/`compactMiddleRange`/`assembleCompacted` + `RunCell.compactMemo`, emits a visible `context.compacted` step, falls back to drop-oldest if the summarizer fails. Tests: `brainRunStore.test.ts`.
- **C — durable tool/memory step visibility.** Tool/recall/learn/reconcile steps rendered live but were in-memory only (`trace`) → vanished on reload. Now persisted (NO migration — `brain_chat_messages.role` is `varchar(16)`, `metadata` free text): `brainRunStore.ts` `pushDurableStep` writes each step as a `role:'tool'` message (`{kind:'step',…}` metadata, result bounded to 4 KB, fire-and-forget, NOT `recordAppended`). `timelineModel.buildSettledTimeline` reconstructs the step nodes from that metadata and DEDUPES against the live trace by `category|label|ts` (so a step in both renders once; a prior run's step, only in messages, still shows). A shared `isStepMessage` predicate (`brain-embedded/src/types.ts`, exported through `@/lib/brain`) excludes step rows from BOTH model-seed builders (`useBrainConversation.ts` — the correctness-critical edit: an orphaned tool message 400s strict vendors), the PRD/summary transcript (`BrainPanel.tsx` `conversationMessages`), and the guest bubble list (`GuestBrainPanel.tsx`). Tests: `timelineModel.test.ts` (5) + updated `useBrainConversation.test.tsx` step-persist counts.

- **Truthful learn step (follow-up, DONE same day — api 2026.7.77 · brain-embedded 2026.7.21 · ext 2026.7.58 VSIX).** The `learn` step was a client-side heuristic mirror of the server gate; now the server reports the REAL gate outcome. `brainEvermindLearning.ts` split into `evaluateBrainLearnGate` (cheap, cached head read → `{learned, version}`) + `dispatchBrainLearn` (the slow coordinator contribution, still `waitUntil`); the dead `learnFromBrainTurn` orchestrator was removed. `POST /chats/:id/messages` awaits the gate and returns `evermindLearn` in the response; `builderforceApi.sendMessages` attaches it (transient, not persisted) to the returned assistant message (new optional `BrainMessage.evermindLearn` / `EvermindLearnOutcome`); the run loop renders the `learn` step off `assistantMsg.evermindLearn.learned` instead of `recalled`. Fixes the false-negative where a connected-but-EMPTY Evermind (recall seeded nothing, but the first contribution still lands) showed no learn step. `reconcile` stays client-side (which recalled memories the answer restated). Tests: 2 new `useBrainConversation.test.tsx` cases (learn shows on server signal with no recall; hidden when server says not-learned).

## ✅ RESOLVED 2026-07-11 — Evermind Validate now uses real SSM-embedding recall (was lexical) (api 2026.7.64 · brain-ui 2026.7.21)

The **Validate** recall preview (and the reply-time grounding it powers, `recallProjectEvermindMemory`) now ranks learned memories by the model's OWN embedding, matching what inference actually retrieves — the lexical TF-cosine is kept only as a graceful fallback.

- **Embedding without an engine publish.** `EvermindLM.forward()` already exposes the final hidden state as `cache.finalX` in the published engine (`2026.7.11`), so new api util `application/llm/evermindEmbed.ts` (`embedTokens` = mean-pool `finalX` + L2-normalise, mirroring the runtime's `MambaSession.embed`; plus `cosineVec` + `packVec`/`unpackVec`) produces comparable vectors with zero engine change.
- **Embed once, at merge.** `ProjectEvermindCoordinatorDO` computes each text memory's embedding with the just-merged model and stores it (base64) on the recent-ring entry; new `POST /recall` embeds only the QUERY and cosine-ranks the stored vectors (per-isolate model cache keyed by the immutable version ref). Legacy ring entries without a stored vector are embedded on the fly. `/recent` strips the vector so the polled inspection payload stays small.
- **Prefer-embedding-else-lexical.** `validateProjectEvermindRecall` calls the coordinator's `/recall`; `method: 'embedding'` (even with zero matches) is authoritative, anything else → lexical `rankEvermindRecall`. The `method` is surfaced honestly in the UI (brain-ui console + web Studio Learnings show a "Semantic recall" / "Lexical recall (fallback)" chip; localized in all 5 catalogs).
- **Latent bug fixed in the same pass.** The prior snippet-size bump (`RECENT_TEXT_CHARS=4000` + `PROMPT=2000` × 30) could exceed the 128 KiB Durable Object value limit and fail merges once the ring filled; retuned to `RECENT_MAX=24`, `PROMPT=800`, `TEXT=2000` (+ embeddings) to sit ~85 KB.
- **Tests:** `evermindEmbed.test.ts` (embedding shape/determinism/normalisation, cosine, pack/unpack round-trip) + `evermindRecall.test.ts` — 31 project-Evermind tests green; api + frontend + VS Code webview typecheck clean.

## ✅ RESOLVED 2026-07-11 — Teaching-metrics sweep CLOSED: quality-weighted learning (#6) + engine siblings (LimbicTrainer grad-norm, video codecMSE)

Final closeout of the "train/adapt/distill computes a metric, then drops it" sweep (the rest shipped earlier 2026-07-11 — Knowledge-Map telemetry, #8, IDE-native #1, engine batch #2/#3/#4/#1-engine).

- **#6 — Evermind learn contribution weighted by run QUALITY, not text length.** The FedAvg sample weight was `text.length`, so a long, failed run taught exactly as hard as a short, merged one. New `finalizeLearnWeight()` in [scoreRunOutcome.ts](./api/src/application/runtime/scoreRunOutcome.ts) maps what's known at run FINALIZE (merged > opened > wrote-files > no-op) to a bounded 0.2–1.0 weight; [cloudAgentEngine.ts](./api/src/application/runtime/cloudAgentEngine.ts) passes it at the cloud learn-text dispatch. On-prem [project-evermind-sync.ts](./agent-runtime/src/infra/project-evermind-sync.ts) drops the char-count for a quality weight (neutral 0.6 default; `contributeToProjectEvermind` sends 0.7 when the run changed files, else 0.4). Floored so the coordinator's `weight>0` gate still lightly learns from a low-quality run. Tests: 3 new `finalizeLearnWeight` cases (api, 11 pass) + on-prem weight assertion (agent-runtime, 6 pass).
- **Engine siblings — PUBLISHED in builderforce-memory v2026.7.12** (git tag `v2026.7.12` → Release CI built + tested + `pnpm -r publish`; all 3 packages live on npm at 2026.7.12; app caret `^2026.7.11` picks it up on next deploy). `LimbicTrainer._clipGradients` returns the pre-clip L2 norm → surfaced via `onEpochEnd(epoch, loss, gradNorm)` (CPU-side, always on — sibling of the GPU trainer's #2). `video-train` now writes `ctx.bag.videoCodecMSE` (was stranded in the detail string, asymmetric with video-roundtrip) and it's in the `runStackDiagnostic().metrics` allow-list. Engine 253 + memory workflow 24 tests green.

Two items initially flagged "view-features" were found ALREADY-RESOLVED on inspection (no work needed, no dead columns):
- **Routing `terms` explainer** — the per-model score-driver breakdown ALREADY exists end-to-end: `summarizeComparison` → `AiImpactInsights.comparison` (per-model `avgScore` + `mergedRatePct` + `ciGreenRatePct` + `avgSteps` + `costPerMergedPrUsd`) → the `ModelRoutingAnalytics` view + `aiImpactWidgets`. That IS "why did model X win"; `computeOutcomeScore.terms` are redundant with it (and recomputable from the persisted raw signals). Not a discard.
- **Worker-side finetune sub-scores** — the ACTIVE finetune-eval path is the IDE-native one (fully shipped: migration 0323 + `AITrainingPanel` chart). The parallel `worker/` pipeline's `model_artifacts` table is **write-only (no reader anywhere in worker/)** and the breakdown is already preserved in R2 + returned to the client, so adding sub-score columns would be pure dead columns. Nothing lost, nothing to build.

BPE merge-stats + RVQ k-means inertia = won't-fix (internal optimization diagnostics, no consumer, invasive signature change; the meaningful codec recon-MSE is already surfaced via `videoCodecMSE`).

## ✅ RESOLVED 2026-07-11 — Incident Management ships end-to-end: Help-Desk/Incident-Manager agent + Freshdesk + on-call + timed escalation + Teams paging + war-room (api 2026.7.71 · frontend 2026.7.48)

A new specialized "manager" and a full incident-management subsystem. A help-desk ticket that reads as an incident is triaged by the seeded **Incident Manager** agent, which classifies which SYSTEM it pertains to, opens a first-class incident, pages the on-call list, and escalates on a timer until acknowledged — updates going to MS Teams + Slack + email and an in-app war-room. Built by reusing existing rails, not new plumbing.

- **Data model (mig `0325`/`0326`) — the BRIDGE.** `incident` task_type + `incident_manager` builtin agent (seeded per-tenant + `provisionBuiltinAgents`). `prod_incidents` (0236) extended into an active response record (`board_task_id`, `affected_system`, `assigned_agent_ref`, `war_room_chat_id`, `escalation_policy_id`/`level`/`last_escalated_at`, `external_url`). New: `on_call_rotations`/`on_call_members`, `escalation_policies`/`escalation_levels`, `business_contacts`, `incident_events`. Each incident mints a bridged INCIDENT board ticket the agent works with the normal lane/dispatch machinery (sibling of the Security agent's SECURITY ticket); `task.incidentId ↔ prod_incidents.board_task_id`.
- **Freshdesk connector.** New `FreshdeskBoardProvider` (clone of Freshservice, same `/api/v2/tickets`), catalog/registry/`CREDENTIAL_PROVIDERS`/connectivity-test wiring, `integration_provider` enum + frontend `PROVIDER_META` + `IntegrationProvider` union. `itsmIngest` now forks incident-type tickets (Freshdesk **and** Freshservice) into `IncidentService.ingestFromTicket` (idempotent by source+external_ref), fires the initial on-call page, and dispatches the agent to triage — opt-in by the tenant having an Incident Manager agent.
- **Agent surface.** 8 new built-in MCP tools (`incidents.open/classify/update/add_note/list/get`, `oncall.page/list`) added to `CLOUD_AGENT_PLATFORM_TOOLS`; `incidentDispatch` + an `incidentTriage` payload marker + a dedicated triage steering block in `cloudAgentEngine.prepareCloudRun` (do-not-code, classify→severity→page→note). The board task's description also carries the triage brief so a general-executor run triages, not codes.
- **On-call + timed escalation + paging.** `OnCallService` (manual/daily/weekly round-robin resolution), `EscalationService` (policies + ordered timed levels; `pageInitial` on open, `evaluateIncident` on the frequent-tick `runEscalationSweep` cron), `incidentNotifier` fans out to **Teams** (new `sendTeamsNotification` MessageCard + `TEAMS_WEBHOOK_URL`) + Slack + email, resolving `u:`/`contact:`/`c:` refs to channels and logging each delivery on the incident timeline.
- **API + UI.** `/api/incidents` routes (incidents CRUD + classify/page/war-room/triage, on-call, escalation, contacts; reads through the read-through cache on `incidentVersionKey`). Frontend `/incidents` page (edge + metadata) with four tabs (Incidents war-room SlideOutPanel, On-call, Escalation, Contacts), full `incidentsApi` client, `incident`/`incident_manager` badges, nav group — fully localized across all 5 catalogs (99-key `incidents` namespace).
- **Verified.** api `tsc --noEmit` + `check:schema` (286 tables, 0 new drift) + `check:migrations` (268 files) clean; frontend `tsgo --noEmit` clean; itsmIngest (3) + builtinMcpService (25) suites green; all 5 i18n catalogs parse with the incidents namespace present.
- **Next (logged in ROADMAP):** live war-room via CeremonyRoomDO (today it's a persisted timeline feed), incident-triage lane-movement guard, agent-as-on-call-responder, Freshdesk status push-back.

---

The manager runs in the background (cron every ~5 min + manual) managing tasks/agents across one project OR the whole tenant, but a human on any other screen had **zero** visibility — activity lived only on the `/projects?tab=manager` feed (which didn't even auto-refresh), there was no toast/indicator, and nothing at all in the VSIX. Fixed by riding the rails that already exist rather than new plumbing:

- **Unified audit (server)** — `runManagerForProject` now emits ONE per-pass event to the unified `activity_log` via `recordActivity` (verb `manager.pass`, attributed to the actual manager agent when one is designated, else system "AI Manager"), so every pass shows in the cross-surface audit timeline / `AuditTrailPanel`. One summary event per pass (not one per scored ticket) keeps the trail meaningful; skipped on an idle pass.
- **One cross-surface live signal** — `GET /api/runtime/attention` (the ONE signal web + VSIX already poll) now returns `manager: { lastRunAt, recentlyActive }`, computed as `MAX(last_run_at)` across the manager's scope (the requested project, or tenant-wide when none) — so it correctly handles a manager scoped to one project OR the whole tenant. `recentlyActive` = a pass within the last 3 min.
- **Web** — self-deciding `ManagerStatusIndicator` in the TopBar (returns null until a manager has run): a pulsing "Manager active" chip while a pass is fresh, else "Managed {relative}", linking to the Manager tab. Reuses `useAttention` (tenant-wide). The Manager tab feed now auto-refreshes every 20 s so cron passes appear live, not just manual runs. TopBar fully localized in this pass (new `topbar` + `managerStatus` namespaces, all 5 catalogs).
- **VSIX** — `AttentionPoller` carries the manager cadence (`managerAttention()`); a right-aligned status bar item shows "$(compass) Manager active" / "Manager · {ago}" (hidden until a pass has run), clicking opens the web Manager tab (`builderforce.openManager`, `appUrl` now exported from auth).
- **Verified** — api + frontend + vscode-host typecheck clean; runtime + manager + token-gate suites green (27 tests); all 5 i18n catalogs parse.
- **Next (logged in ROADMAP):** the human→manager **Coaching Session** (chat with the manager in web Brain + VSIX that turns guidance into manager directives/tasks) — a distinct larger feature, designed but not built here.

## ✅ RESOLVED 2026-07-11 — Teaching telemetry: surface training data instead of discarding it (Knowledge Map + finetune eval + engine metrics sweep)

Follow-through on "shouldn't we be able to train the neocortex?" → "show the data on the knowledge map" → "are there other spots where teaching throws metrics away?". The `evermind` Studio DOES train the cortex (coordinator DO `EvermindLMTrainer.fit` → FedAvg merge → new version); it just hid the numbers. A two-repo sweep then found the same compute-then-discard pattern in several other teach/train paths. Shipped app-side:

- **Knowledge Map training telemetry** — `ProjectEvermindCoordinatorDO.drain()` now records per-version `{ loss, seqs, moved, deltaNorm, merged }` (real trainer loss + honest base→merged L2 weight-movement, new `deltaNorm` on `evermindMerge.mergeCheckpointDiffs`), threaded through `getProjectEvermindContributions().training` → a loss sparkline + Loss/Weights-moved/Update-size readout on `EvermindBrainMap` (themed, responsive, localized `evermindBrain.train*` in all 5 catalogs). Merge test asserts `deltaNorm = √Σ(merged−base)²`.
- **#8 IDE-native finetune eval was FAKE → real judge** — `POST /ide/training/:id/evaluate` (`ideRoutes.ts`) generated paid outputs then hard-coded `score=0.85`; now routes through a real AI judge (`application/finetune/evaluateFinetune.ts`, mirrors the worker judge; uses the `readProxyChoice` unwrap primitive).
- **#1 (IDE-native half) finetune sub-scores now persisted + shown** — migration `0323_ide_training_eval_scores.sql` adds `eval_score / eval_code_correctness / eval_reasoning_quality / eval_hallucination_rate / eval_details / evaluated_at` to `ide_training_jobs`; the evaluate route persists the full breakdown; `AITrainingPanel` renders a durable eval card (localized `aiTraining.eval*Label` + `reEvaluate` in all 5 catalogs) instead of a one-shot log line.

Engine-side fixes shipped in **builderforce-memory v2026.7.11** (published; app deps bumped `^2026.6.39`→`^2026.7.11` across api/frontend/agent-runtime + lancedb ext, installed, typechecks green):
- **#2** `MambaTrainer` reads back the pre-clip grad-norm (opt-in `trackGradNorm`, one small `readBuffer`) → `AdaptResult.gradNorm` (flows through `DistillResult`); the instability early-warning that spikes before a loss goes non-finite.
- **#3** `MemoryStore.recallSimilarScored` carries each hit's true 0..1 similarity → `EvermindCognition.recallDetailed` ranks by real similarity × trust instead of the `1/(idx+1)` positional proxy (`recallSimilar` kept as the score-dropping convenience wrapper).
- **#4** `DistillationEngine` keeps the quality-gate perplexity as `DistillResult.gatePerplexity` on the trained path (was discarded for exactly the exemplars that get trained).
- **#1-engine** `runStackDiagnostic().metrics` returns a curated bag (`trainingHistory`, `datasetMetrics`, `benchmark`, `converged`, `codeBenchmark`, `videoReconMSE`, …) instead of leaving them in `ctx.bag`. **Consumer shipped:** `EvermindBuildPanel` renders a loss-curve sparkline + perplexity/top-1/pass@1/dataset-quality tiles + converged badge (shared `lib/sparkline.ts` extracted and reused by the Knowledge-Map readout; localized `evermindBuild.m*` in all 5 catalogs). Engine build + 364 memory tests green.

## ✅ RESOLVED 2026-07-11 — Superadmin-owned account never freezes: tenant-level token bypass in the ONE gate + Manager "autonomy paused" surfacing (api + frontend)

Diagnosed from "the AI Manager isn't working / Evermind stopped learning ~11h ago while the Manager tab shows last run = yesterday." Root cause: the cron manager sweep (`runManagerSweep`) and the always-on autonomous executor (`runAutonomousExecutionSweep`) both gate on `getTenantTokenAvailability` and skip a token-capped tenant — but that resolver only granted the "superadmin ⇒ unlimited" bypass from `opts.actingUserId`, which the crons don't pass. So a **superadmin-OWNED account** (unlimited by definition) had its board frozen (no rank/assign/dispatch) and its Evermind stopped learning (no runs finish → nothing enqueued to the coordinator DO), while only manual "Run manager now" (which doesn't token-gate) still worked — the exact "works when I click, dead on autopilot" asymmetry.

- **One-source fix** — [`tenantTokenAvailability.ts`](./api/src/application/llm/tenantTokenAvailability.ts) now resolves superadmin from — in order — (1) a caller-provided principal flag `opts.actingIsSuperadmin` (the gateway's `access.isSuperadmin`, covering `bfk_*` key-creators with no user row), (2) `opts.actingUserId` → `users.isSuperadmin`, and (3) the tenant's OWN active membership via the new exported `tenantHasSuperadminMember(db, tenantId, env?)` (indexed `tenant_members → users.is_superadmin`, read-through cached 5-min when `env` passed). Restructured to resolve plan caps first and only consult superadmin (and skip the usage scan) for an already-capped tenant, so unlimited tenants pay nothing.
- **Gateway folded onto the ONE entry — no parallel cap** — `enforceTokenCaps` (llmRoutes.ts) previously re-implemented `resolveTokenLimits` + the usage scan + its own superadmin check. It now DELEGATES to `getTenantTokenAvailability` for the plan verdict + usage (passing the plan snapshot it already holds on `access` via `opts.planSnapshot`, so no redundant tenant-row read on the hot path) and only layers the gateway-specific per-agentHost daily cap on top. So "an account owned by a superadmin is unlimited everywhere" now holds on the HTTP gateway too, and there is a single definition of "out of tokens". The duplicated "Upgrade to Pro/Teams" copy was DRY'd — `tokenGateUpgradeHint` is exported + reused by the gateway. Threaded `env` through `checkTenantTokenGate` + the cron/manager/run/teacher callers so the tenant-owner lookup is cached on every path.
- **Surfacing (for genuinely-capped customer tenants)** — `GET /api/manager/:projectId` returns `autonomy: { tokenBlocked, reason, effectivePlan }` ([managerRoutes.ts](./api/src/presentation/routes/managerRoutes.ts)); [`ManagerContent.tsx`](./frontend/src/components/manager/ManagerContent.tsx) renders a themed, responsive "Autonomous management paused" banner (localized in all 5 catalogs, `manager.autonomyPaused.*`) so a stale "last managed" reads as "out of tokens — only manual runs work", not a silent break.
- **Confirmed NOT parallel** — `meters.ts` + `builderInsights.ts` only DISPLAY limits (reuse the shared `resolveTokenLimits` primitive, no gate); `pendingAgentsUpgradeEmail` consumes the shared availability result; `isPaidOverflowExhausted` is a separate millicents-overflow cap, not the token cap.
- **Verified** — `tenantTokenAvailability.test.ts` (12 pass, incl. cron-path superadmin-owned + gateway pre-resolved-principal cases); `llmRoutes.test.ts` cap suite green (incl. teams-unlimited); `autonomousExecutionSweep`/`evermindTeacher`/`PlanLimits` green; api + frontend typecheck clean.

---

## ✅ RESOLVED 2026-07-09 — Evermind video + image generation: engine codec, Studio build steps, image path, codec serialization (builderforce-memory `2026.7.1`)

Enabled Evermind to generate video/image WITHOUT a new model — the generator (`EvermindLM`) is a modality-agnostic next-token predictor, so this is a codec + vocabulary problem. New `packages/memory-engine/src/codec/`:

- **`VideoRVQCodec`** ([video_rvq.ts](../builderforce-memory/packages/memory-engine/src/codec/video_rvq.ts)) — TEMPORAL residual-VQ: patchify frames → keyframes quantize against an intra codebook bank, other frames quantize the residual vs the previous *reconstructed* frame (closed-loop) against an inter bank → self-delimiting `<vid> … </vid>` token stream. Tolerant `decode` (pads short/noisy streams, never throws). `fit()` learns both banks via greedy per-level k-means. `serialize()`/`deserialize()` ("VRQ0" blob) so a trained codec can ship with the model (the serving-side unblock).
- **`MultimodalVocab`** ([multimodal_vocab.ts](../builderforce-memory/packages/memory-engine/src/codec/multimodal_vocab.ts)) — lays text ⊕ 4 control tokens ⊕ video codes on one flat token axis; `.size` is the model's `vocabSize`.
- **`ImageRVQCodec`** ([image_rvq.ts](../builderforce-memory/packages/memory-engine/src/codec/image_rvq.ts)) — still image = the single-frame (`keyframeInterval:1`) case, a thin DRY wrapper over the video codec.
- **Bridges** ([evermind_video.ts](../builderforce-memory/packages/memory-engine/src/codec/evermind_video.ts)) — `buildVideoSequence`, `generateVideo`, `generateImage` drive the UNCHANGED `EvermindLM.generate`; no model fork.
- **Studio BUILD steps** ([workflow/steps.ts](../builderforce-memory/packages/memory/src/workflow/steps.ts)) — `video-train` (fit codec → build sequences → train EvermindLM; self-runnable on synthetic clips) and `video-roundtrip` (encode→decode reconstruction MSE gate + generate→decode smoke test), registered in the step palette.
- **Self-contained media artifacts** ([moe_package.ts](../builderforce-memory/packages/memory-engine/src/moe/moe_package.ts)) — `EvermindModelPackage.fromMediaLM(lm, codec, {modality})` bundles the VRQ codec alongside the weights in one `.evermind` blob (backward-compatible layout: `checkpointBytes` in the manifest splits checkpoint from codec; text packages are byte-unchanged and carry no codec). `validate()` checksums the codec section; `loadMediaLM()` reloads `{lm, codec, modality}` for `generateVideo`/`generateImage`. The `video-roundtrip` step now does the full deploy round-trip (package→reload→generate, served tokens must match trained) and emits `ctx.artifacts.evermind`.
- **Verified** — engine `tests/video_rvq.test.ts` (14, incl. 3 media-package round-trip/corruption/backward-compat) + 2 workflow tests; full suites green (**engine 253, memory 364**). All three packages at `2026.7.1` (lockstep, unreleased); **NOT** published (`pnpm -r publish` left to operator).
- **Open follow-ups** (in ROADMAP): api `evermind/<ref>` media serving is now HTTP-surface-only (engine artifact prerequisite done — `loadMediaLM` + `generateVideo`/`generateImage`); and the real corpus + GPU training run for coherent output.

---

## ✅ RESOLVED 2026-07-09 — BYO Anthropic resolution: precise failure reason, transient-refresh hardening, and cross-workspace (tenant-mismatch) detection (api + brain-embedded + VSIX `2026.7.54`)

Closes the last P1 of the "should have used Opus" thread — WHY a connected Anthropic account didn't resolve is now handled AND surfaced in code, no live guesswork:

- **Transient-refresh hardening** — `resolveAnthropicResolution` (api `tenantProviderKeyService`) no longer drops the tenant onto the shared pool on a transient OAuth refresh failure (5xx/429/network) while the access token is still within its REAL validity (`expires + OAUTH_SAFETY_MARGIN_MS`, now exported from `anthropicOAuth`). It reuses the still-good token and only gives up once genuinely past expiry. `refreshAnthropicToken` now carries the HTTP `status` on its error so a **revoked** (401/403) token is distinguished from a transient one.
- **Precise unresolved reason** — resolution reports `revoked | expired | undecryptable`; `TenantLlmCredentials.unresolvedReasons` + `formatByoUnresolvedHeader` encode `provider:reason` into `x-builderforce-byo-unresolved` (e.g. `anthropic:revoked`).
- **Cross-workspace (tenant-mismatch) detection** — `providersConnectedInOtherWorkspaces` (one indexed query over the user's OTHER active tenants) surfaces reason `other-workspace` when the SAME user connected the provider under a DIFFERENT workspace than the VSIX resolves. Gated to agentic turns with nothing connected in this tenant, and **cached per user** (`getOrSetCached`, 5-min KV / 60-s L1) so it never adds per-request cost on the common path.
- **Client surfacing (DRY)** — shared `parseByoUnresolved` / `byoReasonHint` / `byoUnresolvedSummary` (brain-embedded) render the reason as an actionable line in BOTH triage copies; the VSIX banner ([`App.tsx`](./clients/vscode/webview/src/App.tsx)) picks "reconnect here" vs "switch workspace" off the reason (`app.byoUnused` / `app.byoOtherWorkspace`, localized in all 5 l10n bundles).
- **Verified** — new `tenantProviderKeyService.test.ts` (11 cases incl. all hardening branches) + brain-embedded triage reason tests; api + webview typecheck clean, brain-embedded 82/82, dist + VSIX (`2026.7.54`) rebuilt.

## ✅ RESOLVED 2026-07-09 — VS Code Brain: BYO Anthropic auto-select, silent-degrade visibility, loop-exhaustion rescue, and read-dedup (api + brain-embedded + VSIX webview)

Reported (VSIX, tenant has BYO Anthropic): a Brain chat auto-selected a weak `deepseek-v4-flash`, thrashed on 62 tool calls into context exhaustion, and errored "The assistant kept calling tools without finishing" — when it should have run the tenant's connected **Opus**. Root cause: the VSIX sent no model (true auto-select) AND the BYO Anthropic credential did not RESOLVE for the request, so `connectedByoVendors` was empty and the coding cascade led with a free coder; the loop then died with no answer. Closed end-to-end:

- **Seed-shadow correctness** — [`LlmProxyService.complete()`](./api/src/application/llm/LlmProxyService.ts) now gates a non-strict caller `model` through `explicitModelPreemptsByo`, so a configured `builderforce.defaultModel`/stale coder pin can no longer shadow a connected flagship (same invariant as `/v1/messages` + `byoAwareModel`). +regression test.
- **Silent-degrade visibility** — `resolveTenantLlmCredentials` returns `configuredProviders`; new `unresolvedProviders()`; gateway emits **`x-builderforce-byo-unresolved`** (added to `Access-Control-Expose-Headers` in [`index.ts`](./api/src/index.ts)). The stream client reads it into `StreamChatResult.byoUnresolved`.
- **Loop-exhaustion rescue** — [`brainRunStore`](./brain-embedded/src/brainRunStore.ts) forces ONE final no-tools synthesis at `MAX_TOOL_ITERATIONS` (mirrors `BrainService.agentReply`); the "kept calling tools" error only fires if that closing turn is ALSO empty. +2 tests (rescue / still-errors-when-empty).
- **Read-dedupe** — an exact-repeat `read_file`/`search_code`/`list_files` call within a run returns an "already returned above" stub instead of re-injecting the full payload; any mutating tool clears the cache (a read after a write is never suppressed). +2 tests. Cuts the context bloat that fed the exhaustion.
- **Account provenance, DRY across both copy surfaces** — shared `formatBrainProvenance(events, {configuredModel, surface})` in [`brainTriage`](./brain-embedded/src/brainTriage.ts) renders `Surface:` + `Account:` + `⚠ CONNECTED ACCOUNT NOT USED: <provider>`. BOTH the web `buildBrainTriageReport` and the VS Code [`transcript.ts`](./clients/vscode/webview/src/transcript.ts) now call it (previously the VSIX copy hand-rolled the header and lacked account/BYO — the "vsix copy missing info" gap).
- **Inline reconnect banner** — the Brain webview ([`App.tsx`](./clients/vscode/webview/src/App.tsx)) shows a passive, dismissable `.bf-notice` (theme-token styled, light+dark) when `useBrainConversation().byoUnresolved` is non-empty, so a degrade is visible without copying triage. brain-embedded 81/81 tests green; api + webview typecheck clean; `brain-embedded/dist` + VSIX webview bundle rebuilt.

---

## ✅ RESOLVED 2026-07-09 — Brain chat live-run indicators: switching chats never stops a run, and every surface shows which chats are executing (VSIX `2026.7.51`, brain-embedded `2026.7.15`)

Reported (VS Code): opening a new chat while one is executing must not stop the prior chat, and executing chats should show indicators in the Sessions list + dropdown. Root finding: the agent tool-loop already lives **module-level** in [`brainRunStore`](./brain-embedded/src/brainRunStore.ts) (a run survives a chat switch by design — switching only re-points the UI subscription, never aborts), so the *behaviour* was correct but **invisible** — nothing surfaced that the prior chat was still live. Closed the visibility gap end-to-end on BOTH surfaces:

- **Cross-chat run state** — new `subscribeRunStore()` + `getGlobalRunState()` on the run store (exported from brain-embedded), returning which chats are `running` vs `awaiting` (paused on a human confirm), disjoint. Fired from the store's existing `emit()`; debounced by callers to the *set* of live chats so it doesn't churn per streaming token. 3 unit tests added (10/10 green).
- **VS Code**: [`webview/App.tsx`](./clients/vscode/webview/src/App.tsx) prefixes dropdown options with `●` (running) / `❓` (needs approval) and posts `runs.local` to the host; [`brainWebview.ts`](./clients/vscode/src/brainWebview.ts) forwards it via a new `onLocalRunsChanged` hook (and clears on panel dispose); [`attention.ts`](./clients/vscode/src/attention.ts) merges a webview-local overlay into `attentionFor("chat", …)` so the Sessions tree lights up local runs with the SAME spinner / ❓ icons + `l10n` tooltips as server-tracked cloud/on-prem runs (`setLocalChatRuns` + `onLocalRunsChange`, wired in `extension.ts`). Awaiting-confirm wins over running.
- **Web parity (the logged follow-up)**: the merge lives in the ONE shared hook [`useAttention`](./frontend/src/lib/useAttention.ts) — it now overlays the client-side run store onto the server attention map (per-chat dot strengthened; a purely-local chat added to `chats` + `counts`). So `BrainPanel`'s chat-row `AttentionDot`s and the `FloatingBrain` badge reflect locally-running chats automatically, no per-consumer change. Frontend `tsc --noEmit` clean.
- The `❓` indicator also resolves the discoverability of a chat paused on a confirm: the approve/cancel UI renders only for the focused chat, so switching away used to hide it — now the row/option flags it so the user knows to switch back and approve.

## ✅ RESOLVED 2026-07-07 — Evermind is now visibly *used and learned from* everywhere: Brain runs on it, per-run chips, VS Code parity (VSIX `2026.7.50`)

Closed the "how do I know any UI is using / learning the Evermind?" gap end-to-end — three features, all shipped and verified (api + frontend `tsc --noEmit` clean; api 21 provenance/teacher tests green; VSIX packaged).

- **Brain chat now RUNS on the project's Evermind (opt-in inference), safely.** The earlier roadmap blocker assumed a gateway change was needed (the gateway hard-pins `evermind/` at [llmRoutes.ts:1318](./api/src/presentation/routes/llmRoutes.ts#L1318), `modelStrict=true`, no fallback). Root insight: `BrainService.agentReply` calls `service.complete()` **directly** ([BrainService.ts](./api/src/application/brain/BrainService.ts)), bypassing that route — so passing `model: 'evermind/<ref>'` **without** `modelStrict` is already a SOFT pin (Evermind seeded at the chain head, capable coding pool follows, cascades on error). The agentic tool-loop stays on the capable model (the tiny SSM can't tool-call); after it produces the answer, if the project head is `inferenceEnabled && version≥1`, ONE final synthesis pass runs on `evermind/<ref>` and is ADOPTED only when Evermind itself served it (resolved model still `evermind/`, ≥20 chars) — else the capable answer is kept. So enabling inference can never blank or break a reply. This complements the already-shipped **LEARN** half (`learnFromBrainTurn`). Gated on the same `inferenceEnabled` opt-in agent RUNS use.
- **Per-reply + per-run provenance chips.** `buildReplyProvenance` now carries `evermind?: {version}` (wire-synced to brain-embedded `MessageProvenance.evermind`); [BrainTimeline](./packages/brain-ui/src/BrainTimeline.tsx) renders a "🧠 Evermind vN" chip under a reply the learned model generated. For agent runs: new shared detector [`evermindRun.ts`](./frontend/src/lib/evermindRun.ts) + new localized [`EvermindRunChip`](./frontend/src/components/agent/EvermindRunChip.tsx) render "🧠 Evermind vN · contributed" in the execution header ([AgentExecutionPanel](./frontend/src/components/agent/AgentExecutionPanel.tsx)) from the run's served-model telemetry + the project head's `connected` posture. (Touching the legacy panel forced its full next-intl localization — new `agentExecution.*` namespace, 39 keys × 5 catalogs.)
- **VS Code parity.** New webview [`EvermindStatusBadge`](./clients/vscode/webview/src/EvermindStatusBadge.tsx) (self-fetches `/api/projects/:id/evermind/head`, host-bundle labels with English fallbacks) wired into the App.tsx chat composer via `associatedProjectId`; the brain-ui teacher-aware teach box + reply Evermind chip ride along. Rebuilt `brain-embedded` + `brain-ui` (tsup) → webview (vite) → VSIX bumped `2026.7.49`→`2026.7.50`, packaged.
- Also confirms RESOLVED: the `EvermindBrainMap` props-refactor P1 (`LlmStudioPanel` now renders `<EvermindStudioCenter>`, not `<EvermindBrainMap projectId>`; frontend typecheck green). New keys: `brainTimeline.ranOnEvermind`, `evermindRun.*`, `agentExecution.*` (all 5 locales).

## ✅ RESOLVED 2026-07-07 — Frontier-model "paid plan only" gates now honor superadmin AND a connected BYO account (api `2026.7.62`, frontend `2026.7.44`)

Reported: the Evermind "Teach from a frontier model" panel (and other "Available on paid plans" frontier gates) blocked a **superadmin** and a tenant who **connected their own frontier account** — even though a superadmin never hits a wall and a BYO tenant funds frontier calls with their OWN tokens. An app-wide sweep found the frontier gates were re-deriving `plan`-only checks with no BYO dimension and inconsistent superadmin handling (`isPaid` in one place, `canChooseModel` in another).

- **ONE shared rule** — `evaluateFrontierAccess` ([planFeatures.ts](./api/src/domain/tenant/planFeatures.ts)): `superadmin || premiumOverride || connected-BYO || paid plan`. DB-touching wrapper `resolveFrontierAccess` + `tenantCanUseFrontierModels` + a `requireFrontierAccess` 402 gate ([featureGate.ts](./api/src/presentation/middleware/featureGate.ts)); the BYO check is the cheapest existing one (`listTenantProviderKeys` — provider+auth_type only, no secrets).
- **Exposed to the client**: `GET /llm/v1/models` now returns `canUseFrontierModels` (folds **superadmin** in server-side, which `canChooseModel` previously missed); `canChooseModel` is unified to the same value. `useLlmModels` surfaces `canUseFrontierModels`; [`ProjectEvermindPanel`](./frontend/src/components/ide/ProjectEvermindPanel.tsx) teacher gate now uses it instead of bare `isPaid` (the run-picker `RunAgentControl`/dashboard already used `canChooseModel`, so they inherit the superadmin fold). Lock copy updated in all 5 locales to name the connect-your-own-account path.
- **Teacher OPTIONS follow their connected account** (the second reported bug — the dropdown showed a free `qwen…:free` for a BYO-Anthropic tenant): `GET /llm/v1/models` now returns `teacherModels` — the tenant's OWN connected BYO frontier models FIRST (a BYO-Anthropic tenant teaches with `anthropic/claude-opus-4-8` etc. on their account), plus the platform premium coders ONLY when the platform funds frontier (paid/override/superadmin — a free BYO tenant must not teach on our premium pool for free). The teacher was fed the plan `codingModels` (free coders on free) and never the BYO models. `useLlmModels.teacherModels` + the panel's `loadTeacherOptions` now use it.
- **Evermind teacher (backend)**: `resolveEvermindTeacherModel` now **BYO-bypasses** the our-pool budget gate (their account funds it); `generateTeacherExemplar` threads the tenant's BYO creds so a strict-pinned frontier teacher runs on their OWN account; the `PATCH …/evermind/teacher` pin route is gated by `requireFrontierAccess`.
- **Deliberately NOT changed**: `voiceCloning` / `psychometricPersona` / `advancedInsights` feature gates — those aren't "use a frontier model" and BYO tokens don't fund them (they already bypass for superadmin via the shared feature gate). Two P3 follow-ups logged (pickCloudModel direct-superadmin; cron sweeps BYO-budget) + two pre-existing test-infra failures surfaced (see ROADMAP).
- Verified: `tsgo` clean (api) + `tsc --noEmit` clean (frontend); new `evaluateFrontierAccess` unit tests + Evermind-teacher BYO-bypass test pass; llm + domain suites green (545).

The `llm` build modality's centre stage is now a live "Knowledge Map" of the project's Evermind, restructured to **form-left / diagram-centre** (`LlmStudioPanel.tsx`) with each column bounded to the pane height and scrolling independently — so the 5-step pipeline rail no longer pushes the diagram off-centre or over-lengthens the page (responsive: stacks under 900px, no 360px overflow; verified dark + light + mobile via Playwright). Closes the roadmap gap "limbic regions are role-only, not live-affect-driven."

- **True SSM/memory anatomy (7 regions), not a generic 4.** `EvermindBrainMap.tsx` renders the anatomy the runtime actually models (from `builderforce-memory` `limbic/regions.ts` + the HybridMamba core): **Neocortex** + **Hippocampus** (memory & reasoning — accrete a live knowledge-node graph from real `/evermind/contributions`: delta runs → Neocortex, taught text + pending → Hippocampus), the **Limbic system** (Amygdala, Hypothalamus, Thalamus, Basal ganglia), and **Personality** (trait setpoints, wired to the limbic regions with dashed "setpoint" edges). Tiered legend teaches the architecture; validated categorical hues + always-visible labels (identity never colour-alone).
- **Limbic regions driven by REAL affect, nothing fabricated.** New `computeProjectAffect(recent)` (`api/.../projectEvermind.ts`) folds the project's real recent activity through the SAME shared `@builderforce/agent-tools` limbic compiler the runtime runs — `deriveLimbicSetpoints` (neutral until a project carries a personality) → `homeostasis` → `appraiseAmygdala`/`appraiseTask` → `thalamusGate`/`basalGangliaExploreBias`. Exposed as `affect: { state, setpoints, attentionGain, exploreBias }` on the (already read-through-cached, version-token-keyed) contributions payload — no new endpoint, no extra DB/DO calls. The four limbic nodes now show live captions: Amygdala "Valence _v_ · arousal _a_", Hypothalamus "Curiosity _c_ · effort _e_", Thalamus "Attention gate _n_%", Basal ganglia "Explore _n_%".
- **Verified.** `api` + `frontend` `tsgo --noEmit` clean on all touched files; 3 new `computeProjectAffect` unit tests (neutral-when-idle, risk lifts caution/arousal, dims stay in bounds) → 17/17 `projectEvermind.test.ts` pass; all 5 i18n catalogs valid JSON with real translations for the `evermindBrain` namespace + `*Live` caption keys.

**Still open (roadmap):** a project-level *personality* would make the setpoints per-project instead of the neutral baseline — today no `project_evermind` personality column exists, so `deriveLimbicSetpoints` receives `undefined` and the affect varies only by recent activity (honest, but the resting setpoint is neutral for every project). Wiring a project personality source flows through `computeProjectAffect` untouched.

## ✅ RESOLVED 2026-07-07 — Personality on task-assignee hovercards (cached assignee-profile source, no per-hover N+1)

The top remaining Personality gap: `PersonalitySummary` showed on `/settings` + the Workforce card but nowhere a *task* names its assignee. The blocker the roadmap flagged was data-access — a naïve hovercard would fetch a profile per card hover (an N+1 across a full board). Closed as one verified vertical slice (API + frontend `tsgo --noEmit` clean; all 5 i18n catalogs valid JSON; schema-drift 278 tables/3559 cols + migration-sequence 263 files green — no new migration needed, the loader reads existing `users.psychometric` / `ide_agents.psychometric`).

- **Cached assignee-profile source.** `loadAssigneeProfiles(db, tenantId)` (`api/src/application/kanban/assigneeProfiles.ts`) unions the two places a personality lives — `users.psychometric` (humans) and `ide_agents.psychometric` (cloud agents) — keyed by the SAME encoded select-value the picker uses (`u:<userId>` / `c:<agentRef>`), returning only assignees that actually carry a personality (small payload; hovercard self-hides for everyone else). Served read-through cached at `GET /api/kanban/assignee-profiles` (`getOrSetCached`, 300s KV / 30s L1) — one tenant-scoped read powers every board card, list row, standup row and drawer.
- **Invalidate on every personality write.** `assigneeProfilesCacheKey(tenantId)` is busted from all four write paths: auth `PATCH /api/auth/me` (invalidates each tenant the user belongs to), and workforce agent **create / update / delete**. Cached-until-written, never stale.
- **Shared components (DRY, self-gating).** `AssigneeProfilesProvider` fetches the map once and exposes `useAssigneeProfile(selectValue)`; `AssigneeHovercard` wraps any assignee name/chip/avatar and shows a **portalled** popover (never clipped by a scrollable board column; flips above / clamps horizontally near the viewport edge; works on hover, keyboard focus + Escape, and tap) carrying the compact `PersonalitySummary` — rendering the trigger untouched when the assignee has no personality, so callers wrap unconditionally. `AssigneePersonalityInline` is the drawer variant (the assignee there is a click-to-edit control a hovercard can't wrap). Both read the same provider map — zero extra fetches.
- **Wired live** into `TaskMgmtContent`: board card assignee (pending-agent chip + human span), list-view assignee cell, standup pivot row headers, and an inline personality readout in the task drawer — all under one `AssigneeProfilesProvider` mounted at the board root. i18n: `assigneeHovercard.{trigger,subtitle}` (with `{name}`) added to all 5 catalogs; also localized two pre-existing hardcoded strings the localize-guard surfaced in the same file (`taskMgmt.bulkChangeStatus`, `taskMgmt.branchAndPr`).
- **Agent card personality parity.** The human `MemberCard` rendered `PersonalitySummary`; the canonical `AgentCard` (marketplace grid + /workforce directory) did not — despite agents carrying `psychometric`. Dropped the same self-hiding `PersonalitySummary` into the `AgentCard` body (reads `agent.psychometric` already on the payload — zero extra fetch), so an agent's personality shows wherever its card does. Fully localized `AgentCard` in the same pass (it had pre-existing hardcoded English): reused `marketplace.action.*` (hire/hiring/unhire/unhiring/workforceAgent) + added `marketplace.card.*` (agentPill, prefers, eval, evalTitle, hired, inUse) to all 5 catalogs.
- **Bonus — API typecheck fully green.** Fixed the last stale pre-existing `tsgo` errors (`reorderPoolForCoding.test.ts` indexed-access under `noUncheckedIndexedAccess`) and retired the now-resolved P2 "6 pre-existing API tsgo errors" gap-register bullet (its other listed errors — activityLog / builtinMcpService / taskRoutes — were resolved by intervening work). `npm run type-check` → exit 0.

**Still open (roadmap):** person-profile page + brain @-mentions personality (drop the same `AssigneeHovercard`/`AssigneePersonalityInline` in once those surfaces mount the provider).

## ✅ RESOLVED 2026-07-07 — Chat tickets/agents 404 "Chat not found" on team & shared chats (divergent access guard unified) — api 2026.7.61

Support ticket: `GET /api/brain/chats/51/tickets → 404 "Chat not found"` while the chat itself opened fine. **Root cause:** two divergent access guards. `GET /chats/:id` (and members) went through `BrainService.canAccessChat` — which accepts both `brainstorm` AND `team`-origin chats (migration 0294) and grants shared-visibility teammates access — so the panel rendered. But `GET /chats/:id/tickets` and `/chats/:id/agents` went through `ChatTicketService.ownedChat`, which silently required `origin='brainstorm'` **and** `userId = owner`. So any **team group chat**, or any **shared brainstorm chat opened by a non-owner teammate**, 404'd on its tickets/agents/messages even though it was plainly readable.

**Fix (DRY):** extracted the single shared-access guard into `api/src/application/brain/chatAccess.ts` (`resolveChatAccess` + the origin constants + `syncPendingMemberships`/`getUserEmail`). Both `BrainService.canAccessChat` and `ChatTicketService.ownedChat` now delegate to it, so a chat that reads also resolves for its tickets/agents/members — no more divergence. Gateway/MCP callers (`userId=null`) keep tenant-wide access; locked chats still restrict to owner/active-member (with pending-email-invite auto-convert). Removed the duplicated guard/`syncPendingMemberships`/`getUserEmail` bodies from `BrainService` and the dead `BRAIN_ORIGIN` const from `ChatTicketService`. `tsc --noEmit` clean on all three files.

## ✅ RESOLVED 2026-07-07 — Workforce/personality gap-register follow-through (OnboardingStepper l10n, engine-column drop, Admin PsychometricEditor, server-backed My Personas)

Four more Consolidated-Gap-Register items across the Workforce/personality cluster, each a complete + verified vertical slice (all touched files `tsc --noEmit` clean — API + frontend; schema-drift + migration-sequence green; the pre-existing unrelated WIP errors in facts/insights/forecast subsystems left untouched).

(The separate child step-body components remain — logged in the roadmap.)
- **Vestigial `ide_agents.engine` column dropped.** The column was written as a denormalized display value but never read for behaviour (the runtime resolves the engine from the `CURRENT_ENGINE_ID` constant). Removed all writers — the workforce create/update raw SQL, the `cloud_agents.create` Drizzle insert, the ignored request-body fields — plus the Drizzle schema field and the now-unused `CURRENT_ENGINE_ID` imports; migration `0321_drop_ide_agents_engine.sql` (`DROP COLUMN IF EXISTS`). Rather than add a redundant `tenant_personas` table (the gap's literal suggestion), server-backed them with the EXISTING `marketplace_personas` table using `visibility='private'` (DRY) — which already flows through the runtime capability path, so a My Persona now reaches execution. Added `PATCH`/`DELETE /api/personas/:id` (owner-scoped, re-slug + Pro-gated psychometric + capability-cache invalidation); added `listMine`/`create`/`update`/`remove` to `personasApi`; rewired `/personas` "My Personas" tab off localStorage (create → POST private, delete → DELETE, publish → PATCH visibility='public' instead of duplicating), with a `serverToUserPersona` mapper + 4 localized error strings; deleted the now-orphaned `userPersonasKey` localStorage helper.

Also confirmed (no code needed): the **first-class member↔role link** the roadmap asked for already exists as `project_role_assignments` (migration 0281) — it is tier-0 (`via:'assignment'`) of the roster fill-matcher; the title/skill/discipline substring matches are fallbacks only. Roadmap wording updated.
