## ✅ RESOLVED 2026-07-06 — Isolation-track parallel close pass (12 small self-contained gaps, skeptic-verified)

Ran the "🧵 Isolation Tracks" as a fan-out workflow (one agent per track, backend parallel / frontend serial, adversarial skeptic verify). Twelve small, self-contained gaps closed with real edits and each independently confirmed present + non-breaking. (Landed alongside the other same-day sweeps in this tree; the `BrainPanel.tsx` + i18n-catalog edits below coexist with concurrent same-day work on those files.)

- **T3 · Agentic Brain chat now prefers a coding-capable pool on tool-loops.** New pure `reorderPoolForCoding(pool)` (mirrors `reorderPoolForQuality`) stable-floats real `CODING_MODEL_POOL` drivers ahead of merely-tool-advertising generalists; wired into `LlmProxyService.complete()` so a request carrying `tools` (and not quality-critical) re-ranks the plan pool toward coding drivers ([`LlmProxyService.ts`](./api/src/application/llm/LlmProxyService.ts) + new `reorderPoolForCoding.test.ts`). Pure permutation — free tenants only float their own free coding models. (The learned-routing tool-loop-success weighting sub-part stays open under Learned Model Routing.)
- **T4 · Dispatch throw no longer strands a run PENDING.** `waitUntil(orchestrate())` now has a `.catch` that re-reads the live execution, and if still non-terminal marks it FAILED, emits a `run.failed` audit event, and calls `notifyDone()` — so a dispatch throw surfaces immediately instead of waiting for the 15-min reaper ([`runtimeRoutes.ts`](./api/src/presentation/routes/runtimeRoutes.ts)); guarded by `isTerminalExecutionStatus`.
- **T4 · `capability_mismatch` is now a first-class Observability event.** `maybeAutoRunOnLaneEntry` emits a task-scoped `auto_run_skipped` tool-audit event (`executionId:null`, category `planning`, detail `{reason:'capability_mismatch', agentRef, missing}`) alongside the existing `console.warn` ([`taskRoutes.ts`](./api/src/presentation/routes/taskRoutes.ts)).
- **T5 · `write_file` tool description made surface-neutral.** The shared schema no longer hard-asserts "opened/updated as a PR on the ticket branch" (false in the local/on-prem editor path); it now describes both effects and instructs the model not to narrate a specific mechanism ([`packages/agent-tools/src/core-tools.ts`](./packages/agent-tools/src/core-tools.ts)). Stops false PR narration on local edits.
- **T7 · SOC 2 evidence JSON export.** New `GET /api/governance/soc2/export` on the mounted governance router — segment-threaded read of `soc_controls` + `soc_evidence`, evidence grouped under each control, structured audit package ([`governanceRoutes.ts`](./api/src/presentation/routes/governanceRoutes.ts) + test). (The evidence-attach **UI** half stays in the roadmap.)
- **T9 · PR-time schema/migration/manifest drift gate.** New [`.github/workflows/ci.yml`](./.github/workflows/ci.yml) runs `check-schema-drift.mjs` + `check-migrations.mjs` + `check-track-manifest.mjs --check` on every PR to main (install-free / DB-free) — drift now fails before merge, not only at deploy time.
- **T1 · Blog SEO.** `blogIndexSchema()` no longer slices the ItemList to 20 (emits every post + accurate `numberOfItems`) ([`structured-data.ts`](./frontend/src/lib/structured-data.ts)); blog pagination is now URL-reflected via `?page=N` (`useSearchParams` + `router.push`, Suspense-wrapped) so it's bookmarkable/shareable ([`blog/BlogPageClient.tsx`](./frontend/src/app/blog/BlogPageClient.tsx), [`blog/page.tsx`](./frontend/src/app/blog/page.tsx)).
- **T2 · Web BrainPanel React.memo now effective + delete dialog localized.** Hoisted the inline `labels` object + render/callback closures into `useMemo`/`useCallback` (with a `timelineCtxRef` for freshness) so `<BrainTimeline>`/`<ChatTicketsPanel>` stop re-parsing markdown on every keystroke; localized the last hardcoded string (the native delete-confirm) via `tBrain('deleteChatConfirm')`/`tBrain('thisChat')` across all 5 catalogs ([`BrainPanel.tsx`](./frontend/src/components/brain/BrainPanel.tsx)).
- **T6 · Voice right-to-delete invalidates licensees' cache.** `DELETE /:id` now collects distinct licensee tenant IDs before the cascade and bumps each `voiceclones:<tenantId>` cache version after deletion, so a deleted clone leaves a licensee's cached (merged) list immediately instead of lingering for the 300s TTL ([`studioVoiceCloneRoutes.ts`](./api/src/presentation/routes/studioVoiceCloneRoutes.ts)).
- **T8 · Marketplace Publish tab + table headers localized.** Every hardcoded English string in the Publish-a-Skill tab, both `<table>` header sets, and the shared row actions routed through the `marketplace` namespace (`publish`/`table`/`action` sub-namespaces) with real EN/ZH/ES/FR/DE ([`MarketplacePageClient.tsx`](./frontend/src/app/marketplace/MarketplacePageClient.tsx) + 5 catalogs).

## ✅ RESOLVED 2026-07-06 — Chat↔ticket auto-link residuals (b) Project-360 taskType, (c) web click-to-open-linked-chat parity, (d) server-side ticket-search typeahead

Closed three of the four "Chat↔ticket auto-link — remaining surfaces" residuals (api `2026.7.59`, frontend `2026.7.41`, vscode VSIX `2026.7.47`; all touched files `tsc --noEmit` clean — remaining API/frontend errors are pre-existing in `reorderPoolForCoding.test.ts` / `MarketplacePageClient.tsx`; `computeProject360` 7/7 tests pass incl. a new taskType assertion). Residual (a) (Retro/Poker sessions as a ticket kind) stays in the roadmap — deliberate.

- **(b) Project 360 `open-task` now carries `taskType`.** Threaded the assigned task's `task_type` from [`computeProject360.ts`](./api/src/application/project/computeProject360.ts) (added to the task select + `Project360Member.taskType` + `Project360Action.task.taskType`, narrowed to `task|epic|gap` via `linkableTaskType`) → shared [`Project360View`](./packages/brain-ui/src/project360/Project360View.tsx) `MemberRow` (into the task action) → VS Code [`project360Panel.ts`](./clients/vscode/src/project360Panel.ts) `Project360ActionMsg.task` → `startTaskSession` (which already derives the ticket kind from `taskType`). An epic/gap opened from a 360 person card now auto-links to its OWN kind, not a generic task.
- **(c) Web click-an-item-to-open-a-linked-chat parity.** New `/ide/:id?ticket=<kind>:<ref>` one-shot deep link ([`ide/[id]/page.tsx`](./frontend/src/app/ide/[id]/page.tsx) `parseTicketParam`, captured + stripped like `?prompt=`) threaded through `IDE`→`IDENew`→`BrainPanel` (docked prop) AND published into `BrainContext` (`initialTicket`, brain-embedded) for the floating drawer. [`BrainPanel`](./frontend/src/components/brain/BrainPanel.tsx) ensures a chat (deep-linked → active → a fresh project-scoped one) then reuses the SAME `brain.linkChatTicket` the picker uses, gating the `?prompt=` send on `ticketReady` so a combined `prompt+ticket` opens ONE linked chat. Real consumer wired: the web [`ProjectHealthPanel`](./frontend/src/components/project360/ProjectHealthPanel.tsx) `open-task` action navigates with `?ticket=<taskType>:<id>` (using (b)).
- **(d) Server-side ticket-search typeahead replaces the load-all picker.** New `GET /api/brain/tickets/search?kind=&q=&project_id=&limit=` ([`brainRoutes.ts`](./api/src/presentation/routes/brainRoutes.ts)) → `ChatTicketService.searchTickets` ([`ChatTicketService.ts`](./api/src/application/brain/ChatTicketService.ts)): a bounded, indexed per-tier `ILIKE` search (≤50, newest-first, empty query = newest page), scoping task/epic/gap/roadmap/spec by project and the strategy tiers segment-wide — fast AND complete on a 20k+ ticket tenant. **Version-token cached** (`ticketSearchVersionKey` + `bumpTicketSearchVersion`, 45s KV backstop); the token is bumped from the central write choke points — `invalidateProjectsList` (task/objective/convert + MCP pmo), `segmentTrackerRoutes.invalidateTracker` (pmo + roadmap trackers, gated), `specRoutes` create/patch/delete, and the MCP `callBuiltinTool` post-mutation hook (`tasks.*`/`specs.*`/`tickets.from_delta`) + `invalidateRoadmap`. The shared [`LinkForm`](./packages/brain-ui/src/chatTickets/ChatTicketsPanel.tsx) now debounces a per-tier `adapter.searchTickets` (replacing `loadTicketOptions` on both the web + VS Code adapters and dropping the old load-all fan-out + 200-cap client filter); new `searching`/`noMatches`/`refine` labels localized across all 5 catalogs.

## ✅ RESOLVED 2026-07-06 — Knowledge & canvas sweep (sell paid knowledge, public browse, content-manager retirement, SOP-grounded diagnostics, legal document typography + version history, Yjs seeding fix)

Most of the "📖 Knowledge & canvas" mega-bullet closed as complete, type-checked vertical slices (api `tsc --noEmit` clean for all touched files — remaining errors are pre-existing in `reorderPoolForCoding.test.ts`; migration + schema-drift checks green; compile unit tests 12/12 pass incl. a new SOP-grounding test). Three items remain in the roadmap and are genuinely infra-blocked / large net-new (hosted-card settlement, block-CRDT canvas + asset uploads, server-authoritative CollaborationRoom + deploy).

- **Sell knowledge in the Marketplace — free + paid, public browse.** Knowledge listings (table `marketplace_knowledge`, "List in Marketplace" via `ListingControl`, `POST /documents/:id/list`) already existed; this pass added the two real gaps. **Public logged-out browse:** extracted the browse into shared [`knowledgeMarket.ts`](./api/src/application/knowledge/knowledgeMarket.ts) (`browsePublicListings`/`getPublicListing`, one cache) served by a new PUBLIC router [`knowledgeMarketRoutes.ts`](./api/src/presentation/routes/knowledgeMarketRoutes.ts) at `/api/knowledge-market/*` (no auth); `KnowledgeMarketSection` now renders for logged-out visitors and prompts sign-in to acquire. **Real checkout:** new `knowledge_listing_purchases` table (mig 0320) + `POST /api/knowledge/listings/:id/checkout`; install is gated on a purchase for paid listings (`priceCents>0`). On the default self-hosted config (`PAYMENT_PROVIDER=manual`) a purchase records immediately → paid listings are fully purchasable+installable; hosted-card settlement is the one remaining roadmap follow-up.
- **`/content-manager` retired → Knowledge.** Content Manager was 100% localStorage (`bf-content-<tenant>`) and the marketplace read that same key. New client-side one-time migration ([`contentManagerMigration.ts`](./frontend/src/lib/contentManagerMigration.ts)) imports each content block into `knowledge_documents` (publishing / listing where the block was), then clears the key; both `/content-manager` and `/content-manager/[id]` are now migrate-then-redirect pages → `/knowledge`. The marketplace `content` category + `loadSharedContent` localStorage coupling was deleted (knowledge listings are the home for sold content now).
- **Diagnostics engine ingests SOPs.** `compileFromDiagnostic` now grounds the compiled improvement agent in the tenant's OWN published SOP/Process docs: new [`recallSops.ts`](./api/src/application/knowledge/recallSops.ts) BM25-ranks `knowledge_documents` (shared `@seanhogg/builderforce-memory/retrieval`), injected via a new `recallKnowledge` dep on `CompileDeps` and wired in `compileRoutes`. Each step is annotated with the SOP it should follow (`config.groundingDocId`) and the SOPs are lowered into `memory.recalledContext`.
- **Legal docs — document-scale typography.** New shared [`DocumentMarkdown`](./frontend/src/components/DocumentMarkdown.tsx) + real `.markdown-body` document typography in `globals.css` (theme-token driven, both themes, responsive). `LegalDocPreview` now renders through it instead of the chat renderer; the knowledge viewer (which already carried `.markdown-body`) gets the same typography and its 3 inline `ReactMarkdown` sites were DRY-refactored to `DocumentMarkdown`.
- **Legal version history + backfill.** New `legal_document_versions` table (mig 0319) snapshotted on every publish AND amend (`legalDocsService`), exposed via `GET /api/admin/legal/history` and a new read-only [`LegalHistoryDrawer`](./frontend/src/components/admin/LegalHistoryDrawer.tsx) (SlideOutPanel) reached from a "History" button in `LegalPanel`. Migration 0319 also backfills historical rows: strips wrapping markdown fences (the SQL of `stripMarkdownFence`) and retires stale "CoderClawLink" placeholder brand text → "Builderforce.ai".
- **Brain-generates-canvas — verified already shipped (stale roadmap).** The `show_canvas` Brain tool (`CanvasPanelBrainBridge`) + "Save to Knowledge" (`CanvasPanelProvider`) already exist; the roadmap claim was stale and was removed.
- **Yjs seeding double-insert fixed.** `useDocCollaboration` now seeds idempotently and gates the timer-seed fallback on `provider.synced`, so a late-arriving WS sync adopts (never seeds on top) — closing the seed-then-sync duplication and staying forward-compatible with a future server-authoritative DO.
- **i18n:** new keys added to all 5 catalogs (en/zh/es/fr/de) with real translations — `admin.legal.history.*`, `contentManager.migrate.*`, `knowledge.{buy,signInToGet,installFailed,checkoutUnavailable}`.

## ✅ RESOLVED 2026-07-06 — Meetings / Live Collaboration gap sweep (external free/busy, tz shading, in-room team chat, chat-scope toggle, VS Code camera handoff, Cloudflare TURN, CeremonyStage i18n)

Six of the ten "📹 Meetings / Live Collaboration" bullets closed as complete, type-checked vertical slices (api `tsgo --noEmit` + frontend `tsgo --noEmit` clean for all touched files — remaining errors are pre-existing in unrelated files; VS Code extension `tsc -p ./` 0 errors). The four that remain in the roadmap are genuinely infra-blocked (SFU app, TURN credential provisioning, agent audio peers, STT for recording) — see ROADMAP.

- **"Find a time" now reads teammates' external calendar busy.** New `freeBusy` method on the `CalendarProvider` interface — Google Calendar `POST /freeBusy` and Microsoft Graph `POST /me/calendar/getSchedule` ([calendarProviders.ts](./api/src/application/calendar/calendarProviders.ts)) — plus a new [`calendarFreeBusy.ts`](./api/src/application/calendar/calendarFreeBusy.ts) (`loadExternalBusy` + `mergeBusy`) that reads **each attendee's own** `calendar_connections` token (not just the requester's), mints a fresh token via `freshAccessToken`, and unions the provider busy blocks into the solver. Wired into both `/api/meetings/suggest` and `/freebusy` ([meetingRoutes.ts](./api/src/presentation/routes/meetingRoutes.ts)). Best-effort per connection + read-through cached (`cal:freebusy:*`, ~2min, hour-bucketed window key) to avoid fan-out on repeated find-a-time. A teammate booked on their external calendar is no longer proposed.
- **Calendar week-grid "your hours" shading is now timezone-correct.** [MeetingsCalendar.tsx](./frontend/src/components/meetings/MeetingsCalendar.tsx) projects each week-grid cell instant into the owner's **declared** `user_availability.timezone` (new `localPartsInTz`, mirroring the server solver's `localParts`) before testing the windows, instead of comparing browser-local weekday/minute — so shading no longer offsets when viewer tz ≠ declared tz. `isAvailable` now takes an instant, not a browser-local (day,minutes).
- **Team chat now rides inside the in-call MeetingRoom.** [MeetingRoom.tsx](./frontend/src/components/meetings/MeetingRoom.tsx) embeds the one `BrainPanel` (`variant="docked"`, `initialChatId={meeting.chatId}`) as a first-class in-room pane behind a header "Chat" toggle — a right-hand column on wide viewports, a full-screen overlay on mobile (`useIsMobile`). "Keep the chat going during the meeting" is now single-surface.
- **ScheduleMeetingPanel exposes the team-chat scope.** Added a "Back with team chat" toggle (seeded from the kind's server default, explicit choice wins) + a named-team `<Select>` (`listTeams()`), sending `linkTeamChat` + `teamId` to `meetingsApi.create` ([ScheduleMeetingPanel.tsx](./frontend/src/components/meetings/ScheduleMeetingPanel.tsx)). Per-meeting chat scoping is now explicit instead of kind-heuristic only. (The scheduler is a `SlideOutPanel`, not a modal — the roadmap's "ScheduleMeetingModal" was a misnomer.)
- **VS Code native meeting webview auto-offers the browser handoff on camera denial.** [clients/vscode/src/meetings.ts](./clients/vscode/src/meetings.ts): the webview's `getUserMedia` catch now posts `media-denied` to the extension host (which raises a native "Join in browser" toast) and renders an inline "↗ Join in browser" button (`open-browser` → `joinMeetingInBrowser` + dispose). A denied in-editor camera degrades gracefully to the always-reliable browser path.
- **Cloudflare-managed TURN credential minting.** `/api/meetings/ice` now mints cached short-lived Cloudflare TURN credentials (`cloudflareTurn`, env `CLOUDFLARE_TURN_KEY_ID` + `CLOUDFLARE_TURN_API_TOKEN`; [env.ts](./api/src/env.ts)) alongside the static `TURN_URL` path — turning "stand up coturn" into "set two secrets". Actual provisioning (setting the secrets) remains an ops step tracked in ROADMAP.
- **CeremonyStage i18n — verified already localized (stale entry).** Audit of [CeremonyStage.tsx](./frontend/src/components/ceremony/CeremonyStage.tsx) found every visible string already routed through `useTranslations('ceremony')`/`('meetings')` (mode toggle, "N at the table", "N live", backlog, drawer copy, `window.prompt` titles, error strings) — the only English left is code comments. No change needed; roadmap bullet removed.

## ✅ RESOLVED 2026-07-06 — Visual Workflow Builder can now author + run a full Evermind BUILD pipeline

The "visual workflow designer can't author a full Evermind build pipeline" gap is closed — the builder surfaces the engine build-steps as node kinds, runs them **in-browser** via the engine, and seeds the project's Evermind from the produced artifact. Smoke-tested against the real engine (`runWorkflow(cloneTemplate('train-llm'))` → `ok:true`, 9 steps, a 99 KB `.evermind` ArrayBuffer + tokenizer vocab 355/merges 95). Every touched file typechecks clean (remaining `tsgo` failures are pre-existing external drift in untouched files — logged in ROADMAP).

- **Palette node kinds** — `nodeKinds.ts` gained an `'Evermind Build'` group with 13 build steps (`train-tokenizer`, `dataset-quality`, `train-model`, `convergence`, `evaluate`, `generate-check`, `benchmark`, `roundtrip`, `export`, `distill-corpus`, `code-parse-check`, `code-eval`, `code-benchmark`), each with typed config fields. The frontend `WorkflowNodeKind` union (`builderforceApi.ts`) is now a documented **client-side superset** — each kind equals an engine step `type`; the server union is intentionally unchanged (build graphs never dispatch through the agentic orchestrator; `roleForNode` got a defensive fallback so a stray server-run can't crash).
- **Graph → engine bridge** — new `frontend/src/lib/evermindBuild.ts`: `compileBuildGraph` topologically sorts the build subgraph into an engine `WorkflowConfig` (parses JSON param fields, drops blanks); `runBuildWorkflow` dynamically imports `@seanhogg/builderforce-memory` and runs `runWorkflow` **on-device (pure CPU, no WebGPU/network)** streaming each step; `loadTemplateGraph` materializes `cloneTemplate('train-llm'|'teach-code')` as an editable wired node chain; `evermindArtifactToBase64` preps the artifact for seeding.
- **Run + publish surface** — new localized `EvermindBuildPanel.tsx` (canonical `SlideOutPanel`): runs the build, renders the live execution-output timeline (pass/fail/skip + ms + detail/error + first-failure banner), and — when the workflow is project-bound and the user can manage Evermind — **seeds the project's Evermind** from the produced blob via the existing `POST /api/projects/:id/evermind/seed`, or downloads the `.evermind`. New `seedProjectEvermindFromArtifact` client.
- **Builder wiring** — `WorkflowBuilder.tsx` gained an "Evermind template…" loader + a "🧠 Build" action (shown when the graph carries build nodes) opening the panel with the live graph; the server "▶ Run" path is untouched for agentic graphs.
- **i18n** — new `evermindBuild` namespace (29 keys) in all 5 catalogs with real translations + ICU plurals; every `t()` key cross-checked present (29/29).

## ✅ RESOLVED 2026-07-06 — Web Brain: gateway float8 500, `BrainPanel` memo defeat, and BYO-threaded summarize/consolidate

Three Consolidated-Gap-Register Brain bullets closed (api `tsgo --noEmit` clean for the touched files; frontend `BrainPanel.tsx` clean — the remaining `ChatTicketsPanel`/`brain-ui/chatTickets` typecheck errors belong to the in-flight `loadTicketOptions` server-side-typeahead work, roadmap item (d), not this pass).

- **Gateway 500 `invalid input syntax for type integer: "0.9"`** — the fix is present and verified in [`api/src/application/llm/tokenUsage.ts`](./api/src/application/llm/tokenUsage.ts): the shared cache-discounted `rowWeight` fragment casts the fractional cache multipliers with `::float8` (`cacheReadTokens * (1 - CACHE_READ_MULTIPLIER)::float8` etc.), so Postgres no longer infers the `0.9`-style operands as `integer`; the caller re-integers the SUM via `clampTokenCount`. This is the token-cap gate the web Brain gateway hits (`sumTenantTextTokensDayAndMonth`). Code-complete — takes effect on the next **api deploy** (ops step, no code work remaining).
- **Web `BrainPanel` defeated `<BrainTimeline>`/`<ChatTicketsPanel>` `React.memo`** — [`frontend/src/components/brain/BrainPanel.tsx`](./frontend/src/components/brain/BrainPanel.tsx) now hands both memoized children referentially-stable props: `timelineLabels` via `useMemo([tTimeline])`; `timelineApplyCode`/`timelineCreateFile`/`renderTimelineMessage`/`renderTimelineStreaming` via `useMemo`/`useCallback` on the stable `hasTool`/`runTool`; and the volatile-closure props (`onAnswerTimelineQuestion`, `renderTimelineAssistantActions`, `onTicketsChanged`) rewritten to read from a single `timelineCtxRef` with `[]` deps — necessary because `useBrainConversation` returns a **fresh object every render** and `recipient` recomputes on every keystroke, so `[conv, recipient]`-style deps would have kept the memo broken. Result: a composer keystroke / streaming token no longer re-renders the transcript or re-parses every message's markdown on web (the same typing-latency win the VS Code webview already shipped).
- **Server-side BrainService summarize/consolidate now honor tenant BYO** — new private `BrainService.buildTenantLlmService(env, tenantId)` builds the internal-call proxy via the shared `tenantProxyForPlan` when the tenant has a **connected account** (Claude subscription/OAuth or a provider api-key → `byoVendors.size > 0`), so `summarizeChat` / `consolidateProjectMemory` / `summarizeAgentHostSession` run BYO-funded ($0 to the operator, on the tenant's own model); with nothing connected it falls back to the unchanged operator-OpenRouter `ideProxy` path, so a non-BYO tenant's background calls never start spending the owner's frontier quota. The three methods + their `brainRoutes.ts` call sites now take `env` instead of a bare `apiKey`. Files: `api/src/application/brain/BrainService.ts`, `api/src/presentation/routes/brainRoutes.ts`.

## ✅ RESOLVED 2026-07-06 — Workforce/boards/kanban/ceremonies/Validator gap-register sweep (AI Manager, kanban.signoff, assignable roster, Validator on-Done, EpicDecomposer LLM, per-agent governance)

A batch of Consolidated-Gap-Register items across the Workforce/boards/kanban/ceremonies cluster, each built as a complete, type-checked vertical slice (all touched files clean under `tsc --noEmit`; the pre-existing unrelated errors in the facts/insights/forecast WIP subsystems were left untouched). `businessValue.test.ts` 13/13 green.

- **AI Manager — fully resolved.**
  - **`source='heuristic'` + `'rice'` path.** `heuristicBusinessValue` now labels its verdict `'heuristic'` (was mislabelled `'ai'`), and a new `riceBusinessValueFromFeature` folds a matching PMO `feature_scores` row into a ticket's value with `source='rice'`, normalized relative to the project's max RICE score. The manager VALUE step matches an unscored ticket to a feature score by normalized name and prefers it over the LLM/heuristic (so a human's deliberate RICE estimate wins and no LLM call is burned). `businessValue.ts` + `ManagerService.ts` (`loadFeatureScoreIndex`).
  - **`manager_ref` enforced as an identity.** New `managerIdentity.ts` resolves a designated cloud-agent manager (`manager_ref='c:<id>'`) into its persona (psychometric profile → prompt directives via the shared `@builderforce/agent-tools` compiler) + pinned model; the persona now steers the manager's business-value scoring, and a `manage` action credits the acting agent in the feed. System/human managers are unchanged (free pool, no persona).
  - **`on_green` PR self-poll.** New `pollPrCiStatus.ts` actively fetches a PR's live combined CI status from the provider and persists it via `setPullRequestBuildStatus`, so `on_green` merges no longer depend on the inbound CI webhook (a repo with no webhook no longer deadlocks; "no checks configured" counts as green). Wired into `coordinatePullRequests`.
  - **Manager/autonomous dispatch dedupe.** The cron manager sweep now SKIPS its step-5 dispatch (`shouldDispatch=false` when `submittedBy='system:manager-cron'`) because the autonomous executor sweep runs the same tick and is the single dispatcher; a manual "Run manager now" still dispatches immediately.
- **`kanban.signoff` + `kanban.audit` MCP tools.** First-class agent-invokable role sign-off (the reviewer round-trip that used to need a hand HTTP call), added to the cloud-agent platform allowlist. The `/api/kanban/tasks/:id/signoff` route now accepts `memberKind='agent'`/`memberRef` so an agent reviewer is attributed correctly; `MCP_VERB['kanban.signoff']='ticket.signed_off'` for the audit timeline. `builtinMcpService.ts` + `kanbanRoutes.ts`.
- **Cached `/api/kanban/assignable` + board lanes sort by `manager_rank`.** New `assignableWorkforce.ts` unions agents (incl. marketplace-**hired**, closing that omission), human members, and active hires into ONE read-through-cached endpoint; `useAssignableWorkforce` prefers it (client fan-out kept as fallback). Board lanes + standup-pivot cells now sort each column by `managerRank` (nulls last, stable) in `TaskMgmtContent.tsx`.
- **Validator agent — on-Done fast trigger (loop-safe) + review-run steer.** New shared `validatorReviewMarker.ts` marks a Validator review run non-mutating; `RuntimeService`'s COMPLETED handler now skips the status transition + lane chaining for review runs (this ALSO fixes a latent bug where the daily-sweep Validator runs knocked Done tickets back to `in_review`). With the loop closed, `recordStatusTransition` fires a fast `triggerFastValidatorReview` the instant a ticket first enters a done-class lane (GAP-excluded, tenant-Validator-gated, dynamic import to break the cycle). `cloudAgentEngine.prepareCloudRun` now consumes the review flag to steer ANY dispatched agent into acceptance-review mode (verify + `builtin_reviews_record`, no code edits) independent of persona.
- **EpicDecomposer LLM `assess()`.** New `llmEpicDecomposer(env)` does real BA-style scope assessment via the free model pool under a strict JSON schema (isEpic + children with title/description/priority), falling back to the deterministic checklist heuristic on any failure; injected at the `index.ts` composition root (was `undefined`).
- **Per-agent governance consumed at execution.** `loadGovernanceContext` now folds `project_agents.governance` (project-specific attachment over the canonical identity row) into the cloud run's context — the per-agent policy was written via `PUT /project-agents/:id/governance` but never bound a run until now.
- **Editable live `swimlane_requirements` + gate.** CRUD on `boardRoutes.ts` (`GET/POST/PATCH/DELETE /api/boards/:boardId/swimlanes/:laneId/requirements`, manager-gated) + `requirement_gate` (off/soft/hard) settable on the lane PATCH — a running board's role/diagnostic/review checks are editable without re-applying a template. Frontend: `boardsApi.requirements` + a collapsible `LaneRequirementsRow` in `BoardConfigPanel` (add/remove/toggle-required + gate selector), localized across all 5 catalogs (`boardConfig.*`, +19 keys each). `Swimlane.requirementGate` + `SwimlaneRequirement` types added.
- **SwimlaneCoordinator (System B) honors requirements.** `launchStage` blocks a `hard`-gate lane while a REQUIRED reviewer sign-off is missing — the ticket parks as `needs_attention` (new `CoordinatorStore.hasUnmetRequiredReviewers`, reading `swimlane_requirements` ⋈ approved `ticket_role_signoffs`) instead of launching its agents; a subsequent approved `kanban.signoff` + retry resumes it. New coordinator test (20/20 pass).
- **`team_members.member_name` drift fixed.** New shared `resolveLiveMemberNames` (three grouped `IN` queries — humans/cloud/host, never N+1) refreshes the denormalized name to the live canonical source (`users.display_name` / `ide_agents.name` / `agent_hosts.name`) at read time in both the project-workforce and team-detail reads, so a renamed member no longer shows a stale snapshot.

Follow-ups still open in the roadmap: `swimlane_id` FK + lane-merge/reassign + per-lane automation flags; multi-hop lane chaining + one status-write notifier; member↔role link; team-scoped/project-scoped pickers; board parent/child tree UI + role-resolved fan-out; `swimlane_agent_assignments`→`agent_assignments` migration; ceremonies internals (JWT re-verify, server `changed`, dnd-kit, pause/resume, power cap, history); personality on hovercards/profile/@-mentions + `tenant_personas` + Admin editor + drop `ide_agents.engine`; template Stripe sales; `OnboardingStepper` localization.

- **Marketplace category deep-link.** The category chip now mirrors the choice into `?category=` via `selectCategory` (`router.replace`, `all` clears the param) so every tab is deep-linkable/shareable/refresh-safe — reusing the same query the existing deep-link read consumes.

## ✅ RESOLVED 2026-07-06 — Per-reply model/account provenance chip: a SUCCESSFUL Brain turn now shows whether the tenant's own connected account served it (api `2026.7.54` + brain-embedded/brain-ui `2026.7.13` + frontend + VSIX `2026.7.45`)

A successful turn revealed nothing about how it was served, so "why didn't it use my paid Claude?" was invisible — `agentReply`'s honest "your connected account was NOT used" note only fired on an **empty** reply. Now every assistant turn carries durable provenance and renders a small chip (resolved model + whose account), across BOTH the streaming BRAIN path and an agent's addressed reply.

- **Authoritative signal, one classifier** — [`replyProvenance.ts`](./api/src/application/llm/replyProvenance.ts): `classifyReplyAccount(byoFunded, hasConnectedAccount)` → `own | shared | shared_byo_unused`, derived from the ProxyResult's existing `byoFunded` (the tenant's OWN credential served it) + whether they have any connected account. One decision, shared by both writers; `agentReply`'s empty-reply "via" note was refactored onto it so the prose and the chip can never diverge.
- **Two writers** — the streaming gateway route emits `x-builderforce-account` (added to the CORS expose list), captured in `streamChatCompletion` (`StreamChatResult.account`) and persisted on the assistant message by `brainRunStore`; `BrainService.agentReply` attaches the same `provenance` to its message metadata alongside `authoredBy`.
- **Shared model + renderer** — new [`provenance.ts`](./brain-embedded/src/provenance.ts) in brain-embedded (`MessageProvenance`, `parseMessageProvenance`, `withProvenanceMetadata`, `PROVENANCE_META_KEY`) is the wire contract; `<BrainTimeline>` renders a `<ProvenanceChip>` on any assistant turn carrying it — `own` (success/green), `shared` (muted), `shared_byo_unused` (warning + "your connected account wasn't used"). Theme-tokened `--bf-*` (light+dark, mapped in frontend globals + vscode webview), responsive, i18n across all 5 catalogs.
- **Tests** — `replyProvenance.test.ts` (5) covers the classifier + builder; api/brain-embedded/brain-ui/vscode-webview all typecheck clean.

## ✅ RESOLVED 2026-07-06 — Brain clarifying questions render as a clickable question card (`ask_user`) instead of unactionable prose (api + brain-ui + both chat surfaces; VSIX `2026.7.43`)

The agent used to ask decisions ("who owns each initiative? create epics under project #11 or dedicated projects?") as plain markdown at the end of a turn; the chat couldn't interpret the free-typed reply and the loop stalled. Now the Brain has an **`ask_user` tool** and the reply renders as a clickable card.

- **Server** — [`BrainService.agentReply`](./api/src/application/brain/BrainService.ts) advertises a conversational `ask_user` tool ({question, options:[{label,description?}], multiSelect?}) alongside the platform tools, and intercepts it as a **terminal turn**: the loop stops and the reply carries a canonical ```ask-user fenced block (`askUserBlock`). A schema-validated tool call is far more reliable than asking a weak model to hand-format JSON in prose (the models in play were exactly the weak free-pool coders). A system-prompt line nudges the model to use it for decisions instead of trailing prose questions. Malformed args emit a corrective tool result (never an unanswered tool call).
- **Shared UI** — new [`askUser.tsx`](./packages/brain-ui/src/askUser.tsx) in `@seanhogg/builderforce-brain-ui`: `parseAskUser`/`stripAskUser`/`serializeAskUser` + a `<QuestionCard>` (single-select sends on click; multi-select = checkboxes + Send). `<BrainTimeline>` lifts the block out of the assistant message and renders the card **before** delegating to the host's body renderer, so it works whether the host uses the default `<Markdown>` (VS Code) or a custom bubble (web) — one implementation, both surfaces. Graceful fallback: no `onAnswerQuestion` or a malformed block → plain text, question never lost. Theme-tokened (`--bf-*`, light+dark), responsive.
- **Wiring** — VS Code webview (`App.tsx`) and web `BrainPanel.tsx` both pass `onAnswerQuestion` (posts the chosen label(s) as the user's next turn via the existing send path) + the two new labels (`askSubmit`/`askAnswered`), localized in all 5 catalogs. Typechecks clean across brain-ui, api, webview, frontend.

## ✅ RESOLVED 2026-07-06 — `search_code` returned false "not found" in the VS Code Brain, sending it into read_file spirals + context blowup (agent-tools + extension)

Symptom (from a triaged Brain transcript, "Review Upwork"): the agent ran `search_code` for `BrainTimeline`, `buildTimeline`, etc. — symbols that plainly exist — and every call came back `{"total":0,"truncated":true, note:"No matches in the indexed codebase — the term is not referenced."}`. Believing the search, the model fell back to `list_files` + large `read_file` calls (largest 54.9 KB, 19 results truncated, 413 KB of tool output), which blew the context window (prompt peaked at 80k tokens) and produced the "keeps searching, nothing gets fixed" loop.

**Two root causes, both fixed:**
- **Depth-first walk in the editor provider.** [`buildLocalCapabilityProvider().searchCode`](./clients/vscode/src/localCapabilities.ts) recursed **depth-first** with a `SEARCH_MAX_FILES = 4000` cap, so on this monorepo it exhausted the budget inside early subtrees (`agent-runtime`/`api`) and never reached `packages/brain-ui` — returning `total:0, truncated:true`. This is the exact bug already fixed for `list_files` (its `walkFiles` was made breadth-first with a comment explaining it), but the fix was never carried to `searchCode`. Rewrote `searchCode` to a **breadth-first directory queue** so shallow files across the whole tree are scanned first; the cap (if hit) now truncates evenly instead of skipping whole subtrees.
- **A tool note that lied on truncation.** [`searchCodeTool`](./packages/agent-tools/src/core-tools.ts) stamped "No matches in the indexed codebase — the term is not referenced" whenever `total===0`, *even when `truncated===true`*. Now the note is truthful: on `truncated` it says the search was cut short (NOT proof of absence) and tells the model to scope with `path` or narrow the `query`; the "not referenced" wording only fires on a complete `total:0`.

**Plus a new `path` scope on `search_code`** (the real fix for context blowup): the tool takes an optional repo-relative subdirectory, threaded through `CapabilityProvider.searchCode(query, scope?)` and honored on all three surfaces — native scoped walk in the editor provider, best-effort path-prefix filter on the cloud (`cloudAgentEngine`) and on-prem node (`node-capability-provider`) backends. The description also now tells the model to pass an exact substring/symbol, not a natural-language phrase (the transcript showed phrase queries like "question response chat render" matching nothing). Typechecks clean in `agent-tools` and the extension.

## ✅ RESOLVED 2026-07-05 — "produced no reply / empty turn" on EVERY model: agent replies never read the response body (+ DRY'd ProxyResult extraction into one primitive) (api `2026.7.52`)

Once the cascade fix (2026.7.51) put the run on the connected account, the reply was STILL empty — now attributed to `claude-opus-4-8`. Root cause, found by re-reading the extraction code: [`BrainService.agentReply`](./api/src/application/brain/BrainService.ts) read `result.response.choices?.[0]?.message` — but `ProxyResult.response` is an **HTTP `Response`** (a JSON body), which has no `.choices`. So `message` was **always `undefined`**, `toolCalls` always `[]`, `text` always `''` — every reply was blank *regardless of the model*. The whole model-routing saga was downstream of this: qwen, then Opus, both "empty" because the code never actually parsed either response. Every other consumer correctly did `await result.response.json()`; only Brain's copies (5 of them) got it wrong.

**Why it existed in 5 places** (the real lesson, per the operator): ProxyResult-body extraction was never a shared primitive — ~12 consumers each hand-rolled `await result.response.json()` + `choices[0].message`, plus THREE separate `extractContent` helpers. Duplication is exactly how one surface rots while others work.

- **One primitive**: [`readProxyChoice(result)`](./api/src/application/llm/LlmProxyService.ts) — THE single unwrap of a ProxyResult's Response body → `{ message, content, toolCalls, finishReason, body }`. Clones the Response (so a forwarded/streamed body stays intact), never throws on a bad body. Its doc-comment calls out the `Response`-is-not-the-body trap so it can't be reintroduced.
- **Migrated ALL 12 consumers** onto it and DELETED the three duplicate `extractContent` helpers (QaGenerator, ArchitectAnalysis, SecurityReview): BrainService ×5 (agent reply loop + synthesis, chat/session summary, project-memory), gatewayJudge, cloudExecutor, businessValueAI, evermindTeacher, classifyTask, compactMessages, SecurityReviewService, taskPrd, legalDocsService, QaGeneratorService, ArchitectAnalysisService. (The dispatch-internal `extractAssistantContent` + cloud-loop `parseLlmChoice` operate on an already-parsed body — a different layer — and are left.)
- **Bonus diagnostic**: the empty-turn message now includes the model's `finish_reason` (e.g. `length` ⇒ token budget spent with no text) so a genuinely-empty completion is self-describing.
- **Regression coverage**: [readProxyChoice.test.ts](./api/src/application/llm/readProxyChoice.test.ts) pins body-parsing (vs reading off the Response), tool-only turns, `finish_reason`, non-JSON safety, and that the clone leaves the original body readable. Verified: `tsgo` 0 new errors; **1655 application + llm-routes tests pass** (two teacher/classifier mocks updated to return a real `Response` + spread the actual module so `readProxyChoice` stays real).

## ✅ RESOLVED 2026-07-05 — THE ROOT CAUSE: the connected account was buried BEHIND the free pool in the cascade composer, so it ran last/never (api `2026.7.51`)

Found by driving the REAL proxy in a unit test (not more speculation, and not the live-API poking that preceded it — that only confirmed the token + request shape are valid, HTTP 200). The reproduction: build the proxy exactly as `BrainService.agentReply` does (free plan + connected `anthropicOAuthToken`, codingOnly, no explicit model) and assert the FIRST model dispatched. It was `minimax/…:free` — **`claude-opus-4-8` was never tried first**.

**Root cause** — [`composeFreeCappedCascade`](./api/src/application/llm/cascadeComposer.ts) built the chain as `[...freeRotated, ...paidSlice, ...premium]`: ALL free-tier models lead, paid trails. The connected-BYO flagship is PREMIUM/ULTRA, so it fell into `paidSlice` **behind the entire free pool**. The free pool (minimax / qwen / `@cf/*`) was tried first, burned through empty-turn responses, and the connected account was reached last — or the run "succeeded" on a junk free model before ever getting there. That is every reported symptom at once ("ran on @cf/qwen", "connected account not used", "produced no reply"). The prior three passes (2026.7.47–2026.7.50) fixed real adjacent issues (base-model shadowing, streaming, timeout class, swallowed diagnostics) but none was the cause — the seed was correct; its POSITION in the composed chain was not.

- **Fix**: the composer takes an explicit `head` — deliberately-seeded leading models (the connected-BYO flagship / an explicit pin) that lead verbatim, availability-filtered but NOT free-capped or reordered. `complete()` passes `seedHead` as the head via `buildCandidateChain`. A cooled head entry is dropped (never force a known-broken model); with no head the legacy "free-first, paid-trails" ordering is byte-identical. One change in the ONE shared composer → fixes the chat surface (and image, for free).
- **Regression coverage** (the thing that should have caught this): [LlmProxyService.byoConnectedAccount.test.ts](./api/src/application/llm/LlmProxyService.byoConnectedAccount.test.ts) drives the real `complete()`→`dispatch()`→anthropic-vendor path with mocked fetch and asserts the connected account is tried FIRST (Bearer OAuth header) and, on failure, is attributed honestly in `failovers` (real status/detail, or code-0 network detail). [cascadeComposer.test.ts](./api/src/application/llm/cascadeComposer.test.ts) pins the head-leads / cooled-head-dropped / no-head-unchanged contract.
- Verified: `tsgo` 0 new errors; full llm suite (480) + brain + vendors green; new composer + integration tests pass. Also confirmed OUT of code, once, that the OAuth token + exact vendor request return HTTP 200 from Anthropic (`pong`) — so the integration is sound end-to-end; the bug was purely cascade ordering.

## ✅ RESOLVED 2026-07-05 — Connected Claude account still cascaded with `(no response)`: surfaced the swallowed transport error + killed the malformed-token code-0 class (api `2026.7.50`)

After the 2026.7.49 timeout+streaming fix the connected account STILL cascaded to `@cf/qwen`, and the diagnostic still said only **`errored (no response)`**. Root re-diagnosis corrected a wrong assumption from the prior pass: **`code 0` is NOT a timeout** — a vendor timeout throws `code 408` ([types.ts](./api/src/application/llm/vendors/types.ts) `fetchWithVendorTimeout`); `code 0` is a *`fetch()` that threw before any HTTP response* (`network: <cause>`). That means the failure is at the transport/request layer, NOT Anthropic rejecting the OAuth auth (which would surface a real 401/403 status). The one string that identifies a code-0 cause — the thrown `Error.message`, captured on `DispatchAttempt.error` — was being **dropped by `attemptToFailover`**, so every consumer only ever saw "no response".

- **Surfaced the real cause end-to-end.** `FailoverEvent` gained a `detail?` field; [`attemptToFailover`](./api/src/application/llm/LlmProxyService.ts) now carries `DispatchAttempt.error` (truncated) into it, and [`BrainService.agentReply`](./api/src/application/brain/BrainService.ts) prints it: a `code 0` connected-account failure now reads `errored (no response) — network: <actual cause>` instead of a dead end. Auth statuses (401/403) keep their "reconnect it" hint. This is what turns the next real run into a definitive fix instead of another guess.
- **Killed the most likely code-0 cause at the source.** A subscription OAuth token (or api key) carrying a stray newline/whitespace makes `fetch()` throw `TypeError: invalid header value` *synchronously* → recorded as a `code 0` "network" failure with no status — exactly the observed symptom. [`prepareAnthropicRequest`](./api/src/application/llm/vendors/anthropic.ts) now **trims** the credential, and an empty credential is raised as a clear `401` auth error (reconnect hint) rather than a mystifying network throw.
- **Tests**: [LlmProxyService.failoverDetail.test.ts](./api/src/application/llm/LlmProxyService.failoverDetail.test.ts) pins the detail-threading (carry + 240-char truncation + omit-when-empty); [anthropicOAuthVendor.test.ts](./api/src/application/llm/vendors/anthropicOAuthVendor.test.ts) adds the newline-trim + empty-token-401 cases. Verified: `tsgo` 0 new errors; llm + brain suites pass (477) + new cases.

> Live verification still required: deploy `2026.7.50`, tag @Ada again. If the connected account still cascades, the diagnostic will now name the transport cause (`network: …`) — a specific, fixable string — rather than "no response".

## ✅ RESOLVED 2026-07-05 — The connected Claude account call was aborting (`code 0`) and streaming surfaces skipped it: fixed the timeout + implemented Anthropic streaming (api `2026.7.49`)

The connected subscription was seeded correctly (Opus) but the run still cascaded to `@cf/qwen` with the honest diagnostic reporting **`(no response)` = code 0** — a network/timeout-class failure, NOT an HTTP rejection. Two root causes, both because the direct-Anthropic vendor was built as a *non-streaming last-resort coding floor* and BYO promoted it to the PRIMARY path:

- **The connected account inherited the free plan's 15s fast-fail timeout.** `resolveRouting` gives a free-plan tenant `vendorCallTimeoutMs: 15s` (meant for throwaway free-pool models). The Anthropic vendor is **non-streaming** — it awaits the ENTIRE completion — so a frontier turn on a big transcript blows past 15s → abort → `code 0` → cascade to `@cf/qwen` → empty turn. Fix: `llmProxyForPlan` now accepts a `vendorCallTimeoutMs` override, and [`tenantProxyForPlan`](./api/src/application/llm/tenantProxy.ts) lifts a **connected BYO** proxy to the premium 60s budget — the tenant's own account is the primary path and worth waiting for.
- **Streaming surfaces skipped Anthropic entirely.** `dispatchVendorStream` skips any vendor with no `callStream` ([registry.ts](./api/src/application/llm/vendors/registry.ts)), and the Anthropic vendor had none — so IDE chat / knowledge-draft (both `stream:true`) seeded Claude then **skipped it**, never using the connected account. Fix: implemented [`callStream`](./api/src/application/llm/vendors/anthropic.ts) — a translator from Anthropic's SSE Messages event stream → OpenAI `chat.completion.chunk` SSE frames (text deltas, tool_use `input_json_delta` → streamed `tool_calls`, stop-reason → `finish_reason`, token usage). Shared `prepareAnthropicRequest` + `throwAnthropicHttpError` so `call`/`callStream` can't drift on request shape or error classification. Streaming also fixes the timeout class for streaming calls (TTFT, not full-completion).
- **De-risked without a live endpoint**: the pure per-event mapper `anthropicEventToOpenAiChunks` is unit-tested ([anthropic.stream.test.ts](./api/src/application/llm/vendors/anthropic.stream.test.ts)) against Anthropic's documented event sequence — text stream (role-once, delta concat, finish + usage chunk) and tool_use stream (id/name open, argument-fragment concat, `tool_use`→`tool_calls`). Verified: api `tsgo` 0 new errors; full llm suite passes (472) + 10 new stream/proxy tests.

## ✅ RESOLVED 2026-07-05 — Audited ALL LLM call sites for BYO drift + consolidated tenant-facing completions onto one base class (api `2026.7.48`)

"Why are there 20+ sites? They should be consolidated as a base class." A full audit of every production `.complete()` / proxy-construction site (24 sites) classified each as tenant-facing (should use the connected account) vs internal utility (operator-key on purpose). It found **10 DRIFT sites** — tenant-facing generative/agentic work still routed through the operator-key-only `ideProxy`, so a connected account was never used there. Fixed by making the correct wiring the ONLY wiring:

- **One builder + one base class** ([tenantProxy.ts](./api/src/application/llm/tenantProxy.ts)): `tenantProxyForPlan(env, tenantId, opts)` resolves the tenant's plan + connected BYO credentials together and returns `{ proxy, byoVendors }`; `completeForTenant(env, tenantId, request, opts)` is the single one-shot path (build → gate explicit model via `byoAwareModel` → dispatch → meter); **`abstract class TenantAiService`** wraps it so a service just calls `this.completeForTenant(...)`. The connected-account logic now lives in ONE place — no feature hand-rolls it.
- **10 drift sites migrated**: IDE chat ([ideAiRoutes.ts](./api/src/presentation/routes/ideAiRoutes.ts)), workforce-agent inference + dataset generation ([ideRoutes.ts](./api/src/presentation/routes/ideRoutes.ts)), knowledge draft/analyze ([knowledgeRoutes.ts](./api/src/presentation/routes/knowledgeRoutes.ts)), the workflow LLM node ([cloudExecutor.ts](./api/src/application/workflow/cloudExecutor.ts)), compile-run ([compileRoutes.ts](./api/src/presentation/routes/compileRoutes.ts)), the PRD drafter ([taskPrd.ts](./api/src/application/prd/taskPrd.ts), `tenantId` plumbed through `ensureTaskPrdRecord`). Two service classes now **extend `TenantAiService`**: [SecurityReviewService](./api/src/application/security/SecurityReviewService.ts) + [QaGeneratorService](./api/src/application/qa/QaGeneratorService.ts). Every migrated site with an explicit model (agent `base_model`, workflow `cfg.model`, compile `runInput.model`) gates it through `byoAwareModel` so a non-BYO default can't shadow the connected flagship.
- **Internal utilities stay on `ideProxy` on purpose** (documented): chat/session summarisation + project-memory synthesis (BrainService), task classification, transcript compaction, LLM-as-judge routing/eval, the Evermind distillation teacher, business-value/RICE scoring, repo-architecture diagnostic, the platform's OWN legal boilerplate — a summary must not spend the owner's frontier quota.
- **`agentReply` consolidated + honest failure surfacing**: dropped its hand-rolled `resolveTenantRouting` + `resolveTenantLlmCredentials` + `llmProxyForPlan` (now one `tenantProxyForPlan` call; the dead `resolveTenantRouting` method + 6 now-unused imports removed). When the connected account is TRIED and cascades off (e.g. an expired subscription 401s), the empty-reply diagnostic now names the vendor + HTTP status ("Your connected Claude account was tried first but errored (401) — the token looks expired or revoked; reconnect it") instead of silently blaming an empty turn.
- **Tests**: new [tenantProxy.test.ts](./api/src/application/llm/tenantProxy.test.ts) pins `byoAwareModel` (the gate every migrated site relies on) across all branches — including the reported `@cf/qwen`-shadows-connected-Claude case. Verified: api `tsgo` 0 new errors; LLM + brain + security + qa + routes suites pass (531). Also fixed a latent `noUncheckedIndexedAccess` error in `legalDocsService.stripMarkdownFence`.

> ⚠️ Superseded by the 2026.7.50 entry above: the OAuth call was still failing as `code 0` (a `fetch()` throw, not a timeout/HTTP status). The failure detail is now surfaced end-to-end and the malformed-token code-0 class is fixed; live re-test pending.

## ✅ RESOLVED 2026-07-05 — A connected BYO account was shadowed by an agent's default base model (Ada ran on `@cf/qwen` despite a live Claude subscription); DRY'd the explicit-vs-BYO rule into one tested primitive (api `2026.7.47`)

Reported: an addressed agent (Ada, Sr PM) "ran on your connected Claude subscription (model: `@cf/qwen/qwen3-30b-a3b-fp8`) but produced no reply" — i.e. the diagnostic **claimed** the connected account but a weak Cloudflare free-coder actually ran and returned an empty turn. Two root causes, both a duplication/divergence of the "explicit-model-vs-BYO" decision:

- **The decision was inlined in 3 places and drifted.** [`BrainService.agentReply`](./api/src/application/brain/BrainService.ts) passed the agent's `base_model` (`@cf/qwen`, a seeded default) as an explicit `model:` pin, which pre-empts the gateway's BYO auto-seed — so the connected Claude flagship never led. [`pickCloudModel`](./api/src/application/llm/LlmProxyService.ts) had the SAME latent bug (a Pro tenant + connected Claude + agent base-model `@cf/qwen` would strict-pin qwen). Fixed by extracting ONE shared rule — **`explicitModelPreemptsByo(explicit, byoVendors)`**: an explicit model wins over the connected account ONLY when nothing is connected OR the model is itself served by a connected BYO vendor (a deliberate pick on the owner's own account). A non-BYO pin (a default `@cf/*` base model) no longer shadows a connected account. Both `agentReply` and `pickCloudModel` now call it — no divergence possible.
- **The diagnostic lied.** `agentReply`'s "ran on your connected Claude subscription" was set from token *presence* alone. Now derived from the model that ACTUALLY resolved (`vendorForModel(lastModel)`): it names the real connected account only when a connected vendor served it, else says "the shared model pool (your connected account was NOT used for this run)".
- **Reply path vs conversation paths — correctly distinct (confirmed, not conflated):** the REPLY path (`agentReply`, an agent acting) threads the tenant's BYO account + tools + coding backstop; the conversation-support utilities (`summarizeChat`/`consolidateProjectMemory`/`summarizeSession`) intentionally stay operator-key + no-tools + no-BYO (a summary must not burn the owner's quota).
- **This should have been caught by tests — now it is.** New exhaustive unit tests in [LlmProxyService.codingPool.test.ts](./api/src/application/llm/LlmProxyService.codingPool.test.ts) for `explicitModelPreemptsByo` (no-explicit / nothing-connected / non-BYO-pin-with-account / deliberate-BYO-pin) and a `pickCloudModel` case reproducing the exact Ada/`@cf/qwen` regression (connected Opus leads, pin ignored) plus a no-regression case (non-BYO pin honored when nothing connected). Verified: api `tsgo` 0 new errors; LLM + brain + llmRoutes suites pass (47 coding-pool, 462 llm+brain, 28 routes).

## ✅ RESOLVED 2026-07-05 — Tagging an agent errored `Agent returned an empty reply`; now runs on the tenant's BYO account with actionable diagnostics (api `2026.7.46`, vscode `2026.7.41`, brain-ui `2026.7.12`)

Directing a chat turn to an invited agent (`@agent`) errored with a bare `{"error":"Agent returned an empty reply"}`, even though the tenant had a **connected, active BYO frontier account** (Claude subscription). Root cause: `BrainService.agentReply` built its LLM via `buildLlmService(apiKey) = ideProxy({ OPENROUTER_API_KEY })` — the **operator** key with `model: undefined` — so it (a) completely bypassed the tenant's BYO subscription/keys and the BYO-leads auto-select, and (b) let the gateway auto-select a weak non-coder for an agentic tool loop, which returned an empty turn.

- **BYO now leads the addressed-agent run** — `agentReply` resolves the tenant's plan (`resolveTenantRouting` → `resolveEffectivePlan`, mirroring the gateway's `resolveTenantPlan` from this service's db) and BYO credentials (`resolveTenantLlmCredentials` → `{ anthropicOAuthToken, vendorKeys }`), then builds the proxy via `llmProxyForPlan(env, plan, premium, { codingOnly: true, backstopModels: CODING_BACKSTOP_MODELS, anthropicOAuthToken, tenantVendorKeys })`. Same BYO-first ladder the Brain chat uses; an agentic tool turn, so failover is restricted to the coding pool. An agent with its own `base_model` still pins it; otherwise the model is left unset so the proxy seeds the BYO flagship (Claude) ahead of the pool. [BrainService.ts](./api/src/application/brain/BrainService.ts)
- **Always-speaks final synthesis** — replaced the last-iteration-only fallback with a post-loop guarantee: if the tool loop yields no prose (only tool calls, or an empty turn), ONE final no-tools completion forces a plain-prose reply. Reduces empties structurally.
- **Actionable diagnostics** — the remaining-empty error now names the account used (connected Claude subscription / provider key / shared pool), the resolved model, and the tool-call/step count, and suggests the fix (retry, set a stronger agent base model, or check the account) — instead of a bare "empty reply". The VS Code webview `authedFetch` now parses `{ error }`/`{ message }` from an error body so it surfaces as a sentence, not raw JSON (the web `throwApiError` already did).
- **Copy reflects tagging** — the recipient picker's per-participant hint is kind-aware (agent → "Replies & acts", person → "Notified"), and the ChatTickets `agentsHint` now reads "Type @ in the message box to tag an invited agent — it replies in the chat and can act on the team's work — or run it on a linked task/epic above" (brain-ui default + all five web i18n catalogs).
- **Verification** — api `tsc` 0 new errors (only the pre-existing `builderforce-quality/server` resolution error); LlmProxyService codingPool suite 41/41; vscode host+webview typecheck clean; brain-ui dist rebuilt; VSIX `builderforce-ai-2026.7.41.vsix` packaged. Live agent-reply on a connected BYO account needs a real subscription + deploy to exercise end-to-end (not drivable in-repo).

## ✅ RESOLVED 2026-07-05 — `@`-mention typeahead: tag an agent OR person to direct a chat turn, in every modality (vscode `2026.7.40`, brain-embedded `2026.7.12`, brain-ui `2026.7.11`)

User (VS Code webview) added two agents to a chat and expected typing `@` to open a picker to direct the message — but `@ada` was inert plain text with no typeahead. The directed-message routing spine already existed (`mentionRecipient`/`resolveRecipient`/`addressedTo` metadata + a "To:" recipient dropdown on both surfaces); what was missing was the composer typeahead UI. Built it ONCE and wired both surfaces so they behave identically.

- **Pure detection helpers (single source of truth)** — [`activeMentionToken`](./brain-embedded/src/directedMessage.ts) (detects the in-progress `@token` at the caret; never fires on an email's `@`) + [`filterMentionCandidates`](./brain-embedded/src/directedMessage.ts) (case-insensitive substring, name-start ranked first) live beside the existing `mentionRecipient`, mirroring its `@([^\s@]+)` grammar. Unit-tested (15/15 in `directedMessage.test.ts`).
- **Shared headless hook + popup** — [`useMentionAutocomplete`](./packages/brain-ui/src/mention/MentionAutocomplete.tsx) in brain-ui owns the token/selection state, returns an `onKeyDown` (↑/↓/Enter/Tab/Esc — consumes the key so it never also submits), an `onSelect` (caret sync), and a theme-aware `popup` node (agents + humans, `Avatar` + kind badge; the CSS-var fallback chain themes it in web light/dark AND the editor). Picking strips the `@query` (the recipient shows in the existing "To:" chip) and calls `onPick` → the host's `setRecipientChoice`, reusing the entire routing spine.
- **Both surfaces, all modalities** — wired into the web [`ChatInput`](./frontend/src/components/ChatInput.tsx) (new `mentionables`/`onMention` props; consumed by [`BrainPanel`](./frontend/src/components/brain/BrainPanel.tsx) passing `participants`/`setRecipientChoice`) and the VS Code webview composer ([`App.tsx`](./clients/vscode/webview/src/App.tsx)). Participants come from `useChatParticipants` (invited agents + active human members) — driven by the chat, not the persona — so tagging works in every modality by construction. Both surfaces keep their explicit "To:" dropdown as the equivalent fallback.
- **i18n + package hygiene** — `chatInput.mention*` keys added to all five catalogs (en/zh/es/fr/de); webview labels follow the existing `t(key, fallback)` pattern. brain-embedded + brain-ui dist rebuilt; frontend + webview typecheck clean (only the pre-existing unrelated `@seanhogg/builderforce-quality` resolution error remains); VSIX `builderforce-ai-2026.7.40.vsix` packaged.


Owner requirement: when an account owner connects their OWN frontier account (Anthropic Pro/Max **subscription**/OAuth, or a BYO api-key for Anthropic/OpenAI/Google), that account must be **used instead of** the free/paid gateway tiers — not merely unlocked for explicit model-picking. Diagnosed from BuilderForce chat #42 (project #11), which ran on `minimaxai/minimax-m2.7` + `deepseek/deepseek-v4-flash` (gateway auto-select) despite a live "Claude subscription connected": the connected subscription (`anthropicOAuthToken`) was threaded into the proxy but only changed **auth** when the cascade happened to land on an Anthropic model — it never **led** the pool, and `byoVendors` was consumed only by the strict-pin gate (so a connected account was used *only when the user picked its model*).

- **One DRY, registration-driven helper** — [`byoAutoSeedModels`](./api/src/application/llm/LlmProxyService.ts) maps a tenant's connected VENDOR set → the owner's OWN premium frontier model(s) to lead with, reflecting **exactly what was registered** (NO hardcoded vendor): connect only OpenAI → GPT leads; connect all three → all three frontier flagships lead, **ordered by catalog TIER (ULTRA→PREMIUM→STANDARD) from data** so the strongest is tried first and the cascade fails over across the owner's OTHER connected accounts before any free/paid model. Per-provider (`providerFrontierFlagship`): Anthropic splits by turn shape — **Opus (`claude-opus-4-8`) for agentic tool-loops, Sonnet (`claude-sonnet-4-6`) for plain chat**; OpenAI → `direct/openai/gpt-4.1`, Google → `googleai/gemini-2.5-pro` (the `direct/`/`googleai/` prefixes route to the tenant-keyed DIRECT vendor, never a bare `openai/…` that hijacks OpenRouter's operator-keyed namespace).
- **Applied on both surfaces** — the gateway completion path ([`LlmProxyService.complete`](./api/src/application/llm/LlmProxyService.ts)) leads the cascade with the WHOLE connected-flagship list when the caller pinned no model (soft seed → the free/paid pool stays as fallback; the strongest head also bypasses vendor-level cooldown), and the cloud-agent pin ([`pickCloudModel`](./api/src/application/llm/LlmProxyService.ts)) leads with the strongest connected flagship (`[0]`) — so Brain chat, on-prem, SDK, and cloud agents ("prefer BYO everywhere") all lead with the owner's account(s). A prefix-aware `isDispatchableSeed` guards the seed list against a drifted flagship constant.
- **Billing correctness (adjacent fix)** — the four paid-overflow computations now key off `isTenantFunded` (subscription **or** BYO api-key) instead of `isSubscriptionFunded`, so a BYO-api-key resolution onto a `claude-*`/overflow id is $0 → byo and never counts against the platform's paid-overflow cap.
- **Tests** — new drift-guards + behavior tests in [LlmProxyService.codingPool.test.ts](./api/src/application/llm/LlmProxyService.codingPool.test.ts) (Opus/Sonnet split, registration-driven multi-provider ordering by tier, OpenAI-only leads with GPT not Anthropic, `direct/openai/` vs bare-OpenRouter routing, every seed dispatchable, `pickCloudModel` soft-seed on free plan, explicit pin still wins). Verified: api `tsgo` 0 new errors; full LLM + llmRoutes suites pass.

## ✅ RESOLVED 2026-07-05 — Gig Marketplace: publish a work item as a hireable gig, MCP-first (api `2026.7.42` · frontend `2026.7.34` · mig `0293`)

"Simplify publishing a project/scope for the Gigs." One coherent slice turning any work item into a bid-able gig, with AI proposal evaluation, meetings tracked against the item, a REAL engagement→project access grant, and the FTE Job-Posting flow — all driven by MCP tools so the Brain can ideate → publish → hire.

- **New hireable work-item kinds + ticket→posting bridge** (mig `0293`): `task_type` gains `product` (a PM-authored product brief) and `design` (a UI/UX or design-review gig). `tasks.hireable` + `job_postings.source_ticket_id`/`posting_type`(project_bid|design|fte)/`engagement_type`/`requirements` link a ticket to its published gig. One-click **Publish to Marketplace** on a ticket ([PublishToMarketplaceModal.tsx](./frontend/src/components/PublishToMarketplaceModal.tsx) + the Marketplace section in [TaskMgmtContent.tsx](./frontend/src/components/TaskMgmtContent.tsx)); the server derives the scope from the ticket so the Brain can publish with just a ticketId ([gigMarketplaceRoutes.ts](./api/src/presentation/routes/gigMarketplaceRoutes.ts) `/api/marketplace/*`).
- **MCP-first**: 11 new built-in MCP tools ([builtinMcpService.ts](./api/src/application/llm/builtinMcpService.ts)) — `marketplace.publish_ticket`/`unpublish_ticket`, `jobs.create`/`list_mine`/`proposals`, `proposals.evaluate`/`shortlist`/`decline`, `meetings.schedule`, `deliverables.evaluate`/`set_status` — all on the cloud-agent allowlist with friendly audit verbs. The Brain composes "project grounded in OKRs" from the existing `projects.create`+`objectives.create`+`key_results.create`. Two new seeded built-in agents (`builtin_kind` `product_manager`, `designer`) via [provisionBuiltinAgents.ts](./api/src/application/agent/provisionBuiltinAgents.ts) + mig backfill.
- **AI proposal evaluation** ([proposalEval.ts](./api/src/application/marketplace/proposalEval.ts) reusing `semanticEval` + a DRY-extracted [gatewayJudge.ts](./api/src/application/eval/gatewayJudge.ts)): the employer AI-scores a bid OR a delivered proposal against the posting's requirements (LLM-as-judge, lexical fallback) → `proposal_evaluations`; 0..100 cached on the row. Bids get Evaluate / Shortlist / Decline-with-courteous-message in [TalentView.tsx](./frontend/src/components/talent/TalentView.tsx).
- **Real engagement access grant** ([EngagementAccessService.ts](./api/src/application/marketplace/EngagementAccessService.ts)): an ACTIVE `freelancer_engagement` is now a scoped grant — the hired worker's [/freelancer/workspace](./frontend/src/app/freelancer/workspace/page.tsx) surface reads the engaged project's board, signals a ticket for review (`request-review` → In Review lane), and presents deliverable proposals (`deliverable_proposals`) the employer AI-evaluates.
- **Meetings against an item** (mig `0293` `meetings.ticket_id`/`job_id`/`engagement_id` + `interview`/`review` kinds): schedule a review meeting (before accepting a bid) or an interview (for an FTE posting) tracked against the exact ticket/posting/engagement.
- Fully localized (`gigs.*` namespace + `workforce.builtinKind.product_manager`/`designer` + nav, all 5 catalogs) + light/dark + responsive. Verified: api `tsc` 0 errors; frontend `tsc` 0 errors; all 5 i18n catalogs valid. Also cleared the transient `gigMarketplaceRoutes.ts` `c.req.json<T>()` narrowing + `Object possibly undefined` errors flagged mid-edit by the concurrent Team-Chat work.

## ✅ RESOLVED 2026-07-05 — ONE unified audit/activity subsystem (api `2026.7.39`, mig 0295)

Collapsed the two overlapping audit trails into a single store. `activity_log` (mig 0287) is now the ONLY audit/activity table; the legacy `audit_events` table + `audit_event_type` enum are DROPPED (mig 0295 migrates existing rows over first: `event_type` → dotted `verb`, `user_id` → human/system actor, `resource_*` → `target_*`, metadata preserved under `{raw}`).

- **The DDD seam is preserved, storage unified.** `AuditRepository` (still implementing `IAuditRepository`) is now an ADAPTER over `activity_log`: `save()` maps an `AuditEvent` → `recordActivity()`, `query()` reads `activity_log` and maps rows back to the `AuditEvent` shape. So its callers (`AuthService` logins/registrations, `AgentService`, `RuntimeService` execution events) and the `/api/audit` endpoint + the `/logs` page keep working unchanged — no route/frontend edits needed. `env` is threaded into `AuditRepository` (index + buildRuntimeService) for cached actor resolution.
- **Readers repointed.** The `audit.list` MCP tool now reads `activity_log` (filters by `verb`/`targetType`); `engagement.ts` counts `activity_log` human/hire actor rows. The 3 hand-rolled `db.insert(auditEvents)` dual-writes in `taskRoutes` are DELETED (the `/next` claim now emits `task.claimed` on the unified stream).
- **Schema.** `activity_log.tenant_id` is now nullable (absorbs the platform-global pre-tenant events `audit_events` allowed); tenant-scoped reads filter on it so a global row is invisible to any one tenant.
- Verified: api typecheck 0 errors, schema-drift + migration-sequence checks pass, api suite **1880 pass** (incl. `RuntimeService.laneChaining` which exercises the audit save path). Also fixed 3 compiler-suggested `as unknown as` casts in concurrent security-ticket WIP that were reddening the whole-program typecheck.

The superadmin `/admin` area was refactored to match the rest of the app and then fully localized in all 5 locales.

Each tab body became a **self-fetching panel** under [frontend/src/components/admin/panels/](./frontend/src/components/admin/panels/) (17 panels) sharing one [`adminShared.tsx`](./frontend/src/components/admin/adminShared.tsx) contract (`useAdminData` hook, `AdminPanelHeader`, `AdminError`/`AdminLoading`, `ModelPoolBadges`) + a single [`EmulationLauncher`](./frontend/src/components/admin/EmulationLauncher.tsx) provider owning the emulate flow (no prop-drilling).

URL scheme `?tab=<group>&sub=<view>` with a reusable inner [`AdminGroupNav`](./frontend/src/components/admin/AdminGroupNav.tsx) pill bar; `LEGACY_ADMIN_TAB` keeps every old deep link working. No capability removed.

ICU plurals + placeholders throughout; the Usage tab's LLM prompt payload was deliberately left literal (not UI). Group + sub-tab nav labels localized too (`nav.tab.admin*`, `admin.sub.*`).

## ✅ RESOLVED 2026-07-05 — Cross-surface session/task live-status indicators (api `2026.7.35` · VSIX `2026.7.36`)

Multitasking across concurrent runs now reads at a glance on every surface: a session/ticket shows **actively-executing** (coral/blue pulse) or **needs-your-answer** (amber flag), from ONE server-side signal, so a session's status follows it wherever it's shown — switching chats on the web never stops the agent executing in the background.

- **One canonical signal.** New `GET /api/runtime/attention` ([runtimeRoutes.ts](./api/src/presentation/routes/runtimeRoutes.ts), after `/active`) returns per-task **and** per-Brain-chat state `{ running | awaiting_input }` + counts. `running` = an execution pending/submitted/running; `awaiting_input` = an execution `paused` on `ask_human` (a pending `question`/`feedback` approval) — most-severe wins. Attribution reuses existing joins (`executions.task_id`; chat via `chat_ticket_links`). Uncached live surface (3 bounded, indexed queries, no N+1 — same rationale as `/active`).
- **Web.** `runtimeApi.attention()` + [`useAttention`](./frontend/src/lib/useAttention.ts) (adaptive poll + project-room WS backstop) + shared self-hiding [`<AttentionDot>`](./frontend/src/components/AttentionDot.tsx) (colours mirror `AgentChip`'s `EXECUTION_STATUS_COLOR`). Wired into the BrainPanel chat-list rows + a FloatingBrain launcher "needs you" amber count badge (visible with the drawer closed). The board already surfaced this via `AgentChip` (paused = amber). New `attention.*` namespace, all 5 catalogs.
- **VS Code.** `bfApi.getAttention()` + singleton [`AttentionPoller`](./clients/vscode/src/attention.ts) feeding BOTH the Sessions and Project & Tasks trees (repaints only on state change; re-polls on project switch / platform write / chat change). Rows overlay a live status icon+glyph — `running` → blue `loading~spin`, `awaiting_input` → amber `comment-unresolved` + `❓` prefix (done tasks now render green). First `ThemeColor` usage in the extension; new `bundle.l10n` strings in all 5 locales.
- **Also localized** the previously-hardcoded `FloatingBrain` launcher + `BrainSignInCTA` copy ("Open Brain assistant", "Meet Brain", the value-prop, "Sign in"/"Create account") via a new `brainLauncher.*` namespace in all 5 catalogs — closing the i18n gap this work opened.
- Verified: api `tsc --noEmit`, frontend `tsgo`, and the VS Code host + webview typecheck all clean (0 errors); VSIX packaged. Board `AgentChip` reused, no parallel state.

Teams can now see and hear each other, not just co-edit a board. Managers can turn cameras on for the whole round-table; anyone can start an ad-hoc or direct call, schedule a meeting, and connect their calendar — for standups, planning, retros or ad-hoc.

Per-user OAuth ([calendarRoutes.ts](./api/src/presentation/routes/calendarRoutes.ts) + provider adapters/[calendarService.ts](./api/src/application/calendar/calendarService.ts)); scheduled meetings are mirrored as calendar events (invites to attendee emails), upcoming events surface on `/meetings`. New env: `TURN_URL`/`TURN_USERNAME`/`TURN_CREDENTIAL` (optional).

## ✅ RESOLVED 2026-07-05 — AI Manager runs are first-class tasks: surfaced, metric-clean, eviction-safe

Closed both residuals logged when the AI Manager "run = a board task" feature shipped, and surfaced the manager's own tasks.

- **Manager tasks surfaced.** The manager overview (`GET /api/manager/:projectId`) now returns `runTasks` — every `source='manager'` "Backlog management pass" the manager kicked off (open / in-progress / done), newest first — rendered as a new **Manager tasks** section on the Manager surface ([ManagerContent.tsx](./frontend/src/components/manager/ManagerContent.tsx)): key, status badge (theme-toned), result summary, owner, updated-time. Fully localized (`manager.runTasks.*` in all 5 catalogs) + light/dark + responsive.
- **Excluded from ALL delivery metrics (no residual).** New shared predicate `notSystemTask` ([application/task/taskScope.ts](./api/src/application/task/taskScope.ts)) — the ONE canonical filter — applied to every task-completion aggregation so system/coordination cards never count: delivery throughput, SPACE, lifecycle + bottleneck (incl. their no-transition fallback), CAPEX/OPEX allocation, workforce/DORA lead-time, engagement, assignee-recommender WIP, project counts (`projectRoutes`), Project 360, ROI, completed-work report, planning spine + `loadTaskCostClassMap`, portfolio rollup, PMO cost-class classify, and the VS Code "my tasks" list. Velocity is clean by construction (points-based; run tasks have no `sprintId`), as are objective/initiative rollups (run tasks have no lineage). The manager's own inline copies were refactored onto the shared predicate too (DRY).
- **Eviction-safe pass.** The grooming pass's per-ticket writes (business-value backfill + `manager_rank` + `score_value` audit rows — 200+ sequential neon-http round-trips on a large backlog, the real Worker-eviction risk) are now collected and flushed via `db.batch` in chunks of 50 (`flushBatched` in [ManagerService.ts](./api/src/application/manager/ManagerService.ts)), collapsing ~700 round-trips into ~14. Scoring/ranking now reliably complete for a 300-ticket backlog in one background pass (the free heuristic fallback already scores every ticket in one pass — the earlier "can't catch up in one click" premise was wrong). The assign/dispatch/audit per-run caps remain BY DESIGN (cost/storm guards), not residuals.
- Verified: api + frontend native typecheck 0 errors (lone pre-existing `builtinMcpService.test.ts` nit, untouched), schema-drift + migration checks pass, all 5 i18n catalogs parse and are in exact key parity.

## ✅ RESOLVED 2026-07-05 — BYO close-out: cloud-compute meter + deterministic non-Anthropic on-prem

Closed the two remaining BYO follow-ups end-to-end.

- **Dedicated "Cloud runs" compute meter.** A cloud run executes on our infra even when the tenant brings their own model (BYO tokens are $0 to us; the orchestration isn't), so cloud usage is now metered independently of token volume. Added `cloudRunsMonthly` to `PlanLimits` (Free 25 / Pro 2 000 / Teams ∞) + `resolveCloudRunsMonthly`; new `application/runtime/cloudRunLedger.ts` (`dailyTenantCloudRuns` / `sumTenantCloudRuns` / `enforceCloudRunCap`) counts distinct `execution_id` on `surface='cloud'` usage rows — no new table, reuses the mig-0284 surface tag. Wired as the 5th meter in the consumption framework (`meters.ts`, `MeterKey`/`MeterUnit` gain `cloud_runs`/`runs`) so it shows in the sidebar `UsageMeter` (☁️ icon, `usageMeter.meter.cloud_runs` in all 5 catalogs, Finance deep-link). Enforced at the ONE cloud choke point — `startDispatchedExecution`'s `!delivered` branch in `runtimeRoutes.ts` — so every cloud entry (Run-now, board, CI-autofix) is gated: over the cap fails the run fast with an upgrade message; on-prem/VSIX runs never touch it; superadmin/unlimited pass; fails open on a metering error. "Shown == enforced" (meter total + gate share `sumTenantCloudRuns`).
- **Deterministic non-Anthropic on-prem BYO.** The `/v1/messages` cascade now HARD-PINS (`modelStrict`) a requested model whose vendor the tenant has connected via BYO, so an on-prem Claude-SDK run on `openai/*` or `googleai/*` rides the tenant's own account instead of silently cascading onto our free pool — mirroring the Anthropic passthrough's "runs on the tenant's account, period" guarantee. A bare/mismatched model stays a soft hint (unchanged).
- Verified: frontend typecheck 0 errors; the new api modules are self-contained and isolated (an unrelated concurrent WIP edit to `taskScope`/`toolRoutes`/`index.ts` was breaking the whole-program api typecheck at close-out — not part of this change). ROADMAP BYO section now has no open follow-ups.
